\doxysubsection{Detailed Description}
The base class for all JUCE user-\/interface objects.

@tags\{GUI\} 

\doxysubsection{Member Enumeration Documentation}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{class_component_a7fd775ea6b1190d5d694fdffa539dfac}\label{class_component_a7fd775ea6b1190d5d694fdffa539dfac}}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{FocusChangeType}{FocusChangeType}}

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{focusChangedByMouseClick@{focusChangedByMouseClick}!Component@{Component}}\index{Component@{Component}!focusChangedByMouseClick@{focusChangedByMouseClick}}}\mbox{\Hypertarget{class_component_a7fd775ea6b1190d5d694fdffa539dfaca350527c976c183a1543958e0698572df}\label{class_component_a7fd775ea6b1190d5d694fdffa539dfaca350527c976c183a1543958e0698572df}}

\end{DoxyEnumFields}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{class_component_af4b602b33a2f82e39560fcffb6a2bd9e}\label{class_component_af4b602b33a2f82e39560fcffb6a2bd9e}} 
\index{Component@{Component}!FocusContainerType@{FocusContainerType}}
\index{FocusContainerType@{FocusContainerType}!Component@{Component}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{FocusContainerType}{FocusContainerType}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily enum class \mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_af4b602b33a2f82e39560fcffb6a2bd9e}{Component\+::\+Focus\+Container\+Type}}\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [strong]}}

A focus container type that can be passed to \mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_a5c6ce0b41244e147db85274cbac0e84d}{set\+Focus\+Container\+Type()}}.

If a component is marked as a focus container or keyboard focus container then it will act as the top-\/level component within which focus or keyboard focus is passed around. By default components are considered \char`\"{}focusable\char`\"{} if they are visible and enabled and \char`\"{}keyboard focusable\char`\"{} if {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_af3618b8c0d0583705db9918f23784833}{get\+Wants\+Keyboard\+Focus()}} == true}.

The order of traversal within a focus container is determined by the objects returned by \mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_a138dc2e3c7f4836d7c127409dab8a56d}{create\+Focus\+Traverser()}} and \mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_a8dc872ef83fedecd89cf814d28236cd0}{create\+Keyboard\+Focus\+Traverser()}}, respectively -\/ see the documentation of the default Focus\+Container and Keyboard\+Focus\+Container implementations for more information. \begin{DoxyEnumFields}{Enumerator}
\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{none@{none}!Component@{Component}}\index{Component@{Component}!none@{none}}}\mbox{\Hypertarget{class_component_af4b602b33a2f82e39560fcffb6a2bd9ea334c4a4c42fdb79d7ebc3e73b517e6f8}\label{class_component_af4b602b33a2f82e39560fcffb6a2bd9ea334c4a4c42fdb79d7ebc3e73b517e6f8}} 
none&The component will not act as a focus container. \begin{DoxyVerb}    This is the default setting for non top-level components and means that it and any
    sub-components are navigable within their containing focus container.
\end{DoxyVerb}
 \\
\hline

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{focusContainer@{focusContainer}!Component@{Component}}\index{Component@{Component}!focusContainer@{focusContainer}}}\mbox{\Hypertarget{class_component_af4b602b33a2f82e39560fcffb6a2bd9eaa306dc83df46675c711fa9863c94dfeb}\label{class_component_af4b602b33a2f82e39560fcffb6a2bd9eaa306dc83df46675c711fa9863c94dfeb}} 
focus\+Container&The component will act as a top-\/level component within which focus is passed around. \begin{DoxyVerb}    The default traverser implementation returned by createFocusTraverser() will use this
    flag to find the first parent component (of the currently focused one) that wants to
    be a focus container.

    This is currently used when determining the hierarchy of accessible UI elements presented
    to screen reader clients on supported platforms. See the AccessibilityHandler class for
    more information.
\end{DoxyVerb}
 \\
\hline

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{keyboardFocusContainer@{keyboardFocusContainer}!Component@{Component}}\index{Component@{Component}!keyboardFocusContainer@{keyboardFocusContainer}}}\mbox{\Hypertarget{class_component_af4b602b33a2f82e39560fcffb6a2bd9eadd6c456358549a13df679cbea4479aea}\label{class_component_af4b602b33a2f82e39560fcffb6a2bd9eadd6c456358549a13df679cbea4479aea}} 
keyboard\+Focus\+Container&The component will act as a top-\/level component within which keyboard focus is passed around. \begin{DoxyVerb}    The default traverser implementation returned by createKeyboardFocusTraverser() will
    use this flag to find the first parent component (of the currently focused one) that
    wants to be a keyboard focus container.

    This is currently used when determining how keyboard focus is passed between components
    that have been marked as keyboard focusable with setWantsKeyboardFocus() when clicking
    on components and navigating with the tab key.
\end{DoxyVerb}
 \\
\hline

\end{DoxyEnumFields}


\doxysubsection{Constructor \& Destructor Documentation}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{class_component_a5ee1827aaa22388d22da5200b70eeeee}\label{class_component_a5ee1827aaa22388d22da5200b70eeeee}} 
\index{Component@{Component}!Component@{Component}}
\index{Component@{Component}!Component@{Component}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{Component()}{Component()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily Component\+::\+Component (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [noexcept]}}

Creates a component.

To get it to actually appear, you\textquotesingle{}ll also need to\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Either add it to a parent component or use the \mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_ad717da76012d971197fd8cf943f3e721}{add\+To\+Desktop()}} method to make it a desktop window
\item Set its size and position to something sensible
\item Use \mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_ac8483af6fe4dc3254e7176df0d8e9f7a}{set\+Visible()}} to make it visible
\end{DoxyItemize}

And for it to serve any useful purpose, you\textquotesingle{}ll need to write a subclass of \mbox{\hyperlink{class_component}{Component}} or use one of the other types of component from the library. \mbox{\Hypertarget{class_component_ae500b88725913a9c7edc6573252eb827}\label{class_component_ae500b88725913a9c7edc6573252eb827}} 
\index{Component@{Component}!````~Component@{$\sim$Component}}
\index{````~Component@{$\sim$Component}!Component@{Component}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{$\sim$Component()}{~Component()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily Component\+::$\sim$\+Component (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [override]}}

Destructor.

Note that when a component is deleted, any child components it contains are NOT automatically deleted. It\textquotesingle{}s your responsibility to manage their lifespan -\/ you may want to use helper methods like \mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_abc8f8338a400c20d5e941ea3a1f67f7b}{delete\+All\+Children()}}, or less haphazard approaches like using std\+::unique\+\_\+ptrs or normal object aggregation to manage them.

If the component being deleted is currently the child of another one, then during deletion, it will be removed from its parent, and the parent will receive a \mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_a2bbc6da3479a1c3f6e711f4caf9edafb}{children\+Changed()}} callback. Any \mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_listener}{Component\+Listener}} objects that have registered with it will also have their \mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_listener_a27203ee2f37fa3e1016ed6f2e3a9cb65}{Component\+Listener\+::component\+Being\+Deleted()}} methods called. \mbox{\Hypertarget{class_component_a8e2e31d288ccd68aae89897d3068f594}\label{class_component_a8e2e31d288ccd68aae89897d3068f594}} 
\index{Component@{Component}!Component@{Component}}
\index{Component@{Component}!Component@{Component}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{Component()}{Component()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [2/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily Component\+::\+Component (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{zconf_8in_8h_a2c212835823e3c54a8ab6d95c652660e}{const}} \mbox{\hyperlink{class_string}{String}} \&}]{component\+Name }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [explicit]}, {\ttfamily [noexcept]}}

Creates a component, setting its name at the same time. \begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_a115ff1bdc3fd5e041e75bce7cbae9049}{get\+Name}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_a64d1ad9a0f8f0d1757e62ac738b36b35}{set\+Name}} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}


\doxysubsection{Member Function Documentation}

\index{Component@{Component}!addAndMakeVisible@{addAndMakeVisible}}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{addAndMakeVisible()}{addAndMakeVisible()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{png_8h_aa8c59027f9ab2769342f248709d68d17}{void}} Component\+::add\+And\+Make\+Visible (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{class_component}{Component}} \&}]{child,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group__juce__audio__plugin__client-_unity_ga966b05a42d98c7296097e073c627dcd0}{int}}}]{z\+Order = {\ttfamily -\/1} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Adds a child component to this one, and also makes the child visible if it isn\textquotesingle{}t already.

This is the same as calling set\+Visible (true) on the child and then \mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_a3340a63ebd9f3a9df41bc0e8fbe3bf0c}{add\+Child\+Component()}}. See \mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_a3340a63ebd9f3a9df41bc0e8fbe3bf0c}{add\+Child\+Component()}} for more details.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em child} & the new component to add. If the component passed-\/in is already the child of another component, it\textquotesingle{}ll first be removed from its current parent. \\
\hline
{\em z\+Order} & The index in the child-\/list at which this component should be inserted. A value of -\/1 will insert it in front of the others, 0 is the back. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{class_component_a909c90277e8e95db68001a94e06b83bc}\label{class_component_a909c90277e8e95db68001a94e06b83bc}}

Adds a child component to this one, and also makes the child visible if it isn\textquotesingle{}t already.

This is the same as calling set\+Visible (true) on the child and then \mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_a3340a63ebd9f3a9df41bc0e8fbe3bf0c}{add\+Child\+Component()}}. See \mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_a3340a63ebd9f3a9df41bc0e8fbe3bf0c}{add\+Child\+Component()}} for more details.

\index{Component@{Component}!addChildAndSetID@{addChildAndSetID}}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{addChildAndSetID()}{addChildAndSetID()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{png_8h_aa8c59027f9ab2769342f248709d68d17}{void}} Component\+::add\+Child\+And\+Set\+ID (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{class_component}{Component}} $\ast$}]{child,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{zconf_8in_8h_a2c212835823e3c54a8ab6d95c652660e}{const}} \mbox{\hyperlink{class_string}{String}} \&}]{component\+ID }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Adds a child component to this one, makes it visible, and sets its component ID. \begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_a909c90277e8e95db68001a94e06b83bc}{add\+And\+Make\+Visible}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_a3340a63ebd9f3a9df41bc0e8fbe3bf0c}{add\+Child\+Component}} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{class_component_ad3cdf7ff7e9c595a25f3a4427e1a222e}\label{class_component_ad3cdf7ff7e9c595a25f3a4427e1a222e}} 
\index{Component@{Component}!addChildComponent@{addChildComponent}}
\index{addChildComponent@{addChildComponent}!Component@{Component}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{addChildComponent()}{addChildComponent()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{png_8h_aa8c59027f9ab2769342f248709d68d17}{void}} Component\+::add\+Child\+Component (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{class_component}{Component}} \&}]{child,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group__juce__audio__plugin__client-_unity_ga966b05a42d98c7296097e073c627dcd0}{int}}}]{z\+Order = {\ttfamily -\/1} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Adds a child component to this one.

Adding a child component does not mean that the component will own or delete the child -\/ it\textquotesingle{}s your responsibility to delete the component. Note that it\textquotesingle{}s safe to delete a component without first removing it from its parent -\/ doing so will automatically remove it and send out the appropriate notifications before the deletion completes.

If the child is already a child of this component, then no action will be taken, and its z-\/order will be left unchanged.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em child} & the new component to add. If the component passed-\/in is already the child of another component, it\textquotesingle{}ll first be removed from its current parent. \\
\hline
{\em z\+Order} & The index in the child-\/list at which this component should be inserted. A value of -\/1 will insert it in front of the others, 0 is the back. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\end{DoxySeeAlso}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{class_component_a3340a63ebd9f3a9df41bc0e8fbe3bf0c}\label{class_component_a3340a63ebd9f3a9df41bc0e8fbe3bf0c}} 
\index{Component@{Component}!addChildComponent@{addChildComponent}}
\index{addChildComponent@{addChildComponent}!Component@{Component}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{addChildComponent()}{addChildComponent()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [2/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{png_8h_aa8c59027f9ab2769342f248709d68d17}{void}} Component\+::add\+Child\+Component (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{class_component}{Component}} $\ast$}]{child,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group__juce__audio__plugin__client-_unity_ga966b05a42d98c7296097e073c627dcd0}{int}}}]{z\+Order = {\ttfamily -\/1} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Adds a child component to this one.

Adding a child component does not mean that the component will own or delete the child -\/ it\textquotesingle{}s your responsibility to delete the component. Note that it\textquotesingle{}s safe to delete a component without first removing it from its parent -\/ doing so will automatically remove it and send out the appropriate notifications before the deletion completes.

If the child is already a child of this component, then no action will be taken, and its z-\/order will be left unchanged.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em child} & the new component to add. If the component passed-\/in is already the child of another component, it\textquotesingle{}ll first be removed from its current parent. \\
\hline
{\em z\+Order} & The index in the child-\/list at which this component should be inserted. A value of -\/1 will insert it in front of the others, 0 is the back. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{png_8h_aa8c59027f9ab2769342f248709d68d17}{void}} Component\+::add\+Component\+Listener (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_listener}{Component\+Listener}} $\ast$}]{new\+Listener }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Adds a listener to be told about changes to the component hierarchy or position.

\mbox{\hyperlink{class_component}{Component}} listeners get called when this component\textquotesingle{}s size, position or children change -\/ see the \mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_listener}{Component\+Listener}} class for more details.

\index{Component@{Component}!addKeyListener@{addKeyListener}}
\index{addKeyListener@{addKeyListener}!Component@{Component}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{addKeyListener()}{addKeyListener()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{png_8h_aa8c59027f9ab2769342f248709d68d17}{void}} Component\+::add\+Key\+Listener (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{class_key_listener}{Key\+Listener}} $\ast$}]{new\+Listener }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Adds a listener that wants to hear about keypresses that this component receives.

The listeners that are registered with a component are called by its \mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_ab063a5c631854864da09106abec78a86}{key\+Pressed()}} or \mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_aeff4d2fdbae4d5974e43b62ab3c304f9}{key\+State\+Changed()}} methods (assuming these haven\textquotesingle{}t been overridden to do something else).

If you add an object as a key listener, be careful to remove it when the object is deleted, or the component will be left with a dangling pointer.

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_ab063a5c631854864da09106abec78a86}{key\+Pressed}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_aeff4d2fdbae4d5974e43b62ab3c304f9}{key\+State\+Changed}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_a5287496e233768c197ad8d74484a85fc}{remove\+Key\+Listener}} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{class_component_ae45db6bb7d7826eb7e936c21fec105ce}\label{class_component_ae45db6bb7d7826eb7e936c21fec105ce}} 
\index{Component@{Component}!addMouseListener@{addMouseListener}}
\index{addMouseListener@{addMouseListener}!Component@{Component}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{addMouseListener()}{addMouseListener()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{png_8h_aa8c59027f9ab2769342f248709d68d17}{void}} Component\+::add\+Mouse\+Listener (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{class_mouse_listener}{Mouse\+Listener}} $\ast$}]{new\+Listener,  }\item[{bool}]{wants\+Events\+For\+All\+Nested\+Child\+Components }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Registers a listener to be told when mouse events occur in this component.

If you need to get informed about mouse events in a component but can\textquotesingle{}t or don\textquotesingle{}t want to override its methods, you can attach any number of listeners to the component, and these will get told about the events in addition to the component\textquotesingle{}s own callbacks being called.

Note that a \mbox{\hyperlink{class_mouse_listener}{Mouse\+Listener}} can also be attached to more than one component.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em new\+Listener} & the listener to register \\
\hline
{\em wants\+Events\+For\+All\+Nested\+Child\+Components} & if true, the listener will receive callbacks for events that happen to any child component within this component, including deeply-\/nested child components. If false, it will only be told about events that this component handles. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\mbox{\hyperlink{class_mouse_listener}{Mouse\+Listener}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_a423c89ca5c8622712202c30cb7a5a69c}{remove\+Mouse\+Listener}} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{class_component_ad717da76012d971197fd8cf943f3e721}\label{class_component_ad717da76012d971197fd8cf943f3e721}} 
\index{Component@{Component}!addToDesktop@{addToDesktop}}
\index{addToDesktop@{addToDesktop}!Component@{Component}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{addToDesktop()}{addToDesktop()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily virtual \mbox{\hyperlink{png_8h_aa8c59027f9ab2769342f248709d68d17}{void}} Component\+::add\+To\+Desktop (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group__juce__audio__plugin__client-_unity_ga966b05a42d98c7296097e073c627dcd0}{int}}}]{window\+Style\+Flags,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{png_8h_aa8c59027f9ab2769342f248709d68d17}{void}} $\ast$}]{native\+Window\+To\+Attach\+To = {\ttfamily nullptr} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [virtual]}}

Makes this component appear as a window on the desktop.

Note that before calling this, you should make sure that the component\textquotesingle{}s opacity is set correctly using \mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_a7320d543cba40183c894474ab78798ea}{set\+Opaque()}}. If the component is non-\/opaque, the windowing system will try to create a special transparent window for it, which will generally take a lot more CPU to operate (and might not even be possible on some platforms).

If the component is inside a parent component at the time this method is called, it will first be removed from that parent. Likewise if a component is on the desktop and is subsequently added to another component, it\textquotesingle{}ll be removed from the desktop.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em window\+Style\+Flags} & a combination of the flags specified in the \mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_peer_a94a21f91c61f8211774d6f43243a6ddc}{Component\+Peer\+::\+Style\+Flags}} enum, which define the window\textquotesingle{}s characteristics. \\
\hline
{\em native\+Window\+To\+Attach\+To} & this allows an OS object to be passed-\/in as the window in which the juce component should place itself. On Windows, this would be a HWND, a HIView\+Ref on the Mac. Not necessarily supported on all platforms, and best left as 0 unless you know what you\textquotesingle{}re doing. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_a3eb22f7e39f71fdad3e84a8700807a82}{remove\+From\+Desktop}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_a854420c3141bb90e440af6c7bc1bd360}{is\+On\+Desktop}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_a543e70d5a3ff75cc3facb476f4cdb131}{user\+Tried\+To\+Close\+Window}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_a6a137109881ef1e268ee5ec51a633269}{get\+Peer}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_peer_aa9732a41b884d1e8021c69908ed72fdb}{Component\+Peer\+::set\+Minimised}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_peer_a94a21f91c61f8211774d6f43243a6ddc}{Component\+Peer\+::\+Style\+Flags}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_peer_a47edec896c72e39f36e1be2bc03659cf}{Component\+Peer\+::get\+Style\+Flags}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_peer_ae14a735045acf686a945392d29cb1b2b}{Component\+Peer\+::set\+Full\+Screen}} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}

\mbox{\Hypertarget{class_component_af83c72f9c98476811522ba8cad855003}\label{class_component_af83c72f9c98476811522ba8cad855003}}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily virtual \mbox{\hyperlink{png_8h_aa8c59027f9ab2769342f248709d68d17}{void}} Component\+::alpha\+Changed (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [virtual]}}

If you override this, you should also invoke the base class\textquotesingle{}s implementation during your overridden function, as it performs some repainting behaviour. \mbox{\Hypertarget{class_component_a54a125231707956e740b295f2622787b}\label{class_component_a54a125231707956e740b295f2622787b}} 
\index{Component@{Component}!beginDragAutoRepeat@{beginDragAutoRepeat}}
\index{beginDragAutoRepeat@{beginDragAutoRepeat}!Component@{Component}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{beginDragAutoRepeat()}{beginDragAutoRepeat()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily static \mbox{\hyperlink{png_8h_aa8c59027f9ab2769342f248709d68d17}{void}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group__juce__core-system_gaf0b3f78ca801d88a7912f4c6bbf50e58}{JUCE\+\_\+\+CALLTYPE}} Component\+::begin\+Drag\+Auto\+Repeat (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group__juce__audio__plugin__client-_unity_ga966b05a42d98c7296097e073c627dcd0}{int}}}]{milliseconds\+Between\+Callbacks }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [static]}}

Ensures that a non-\/stop stream of mouse-\/drag events will be sent during the current mouse-\/drag operation.

This allows you to make sure that \mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_aff01e4d339bda474a66984b709044b63}{mouse\+Drag()}} events are sent continuously, even when the mouse isn\textquotesingle{}t moving. This can be useful for things like auto-\/scrolling components when the mouse is near an edge.

Call this method during a \mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_a2a908e064b0bfed1ea0a75b0a0fee6dd}{mouse\+Down()}} or \mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_aff01e4d339bda474a66984b709044b63}{mouse\+Drag()}} callback, specifying the minimum interval between consecutive mouse drag callbacks. The callbacks will continue until the mouse is released, and then the interval will be reset, so you need to make sure it\textquotesingle{}s called every time you begin a drag event. Passing an interval of 0 or less will cancel the auto-\/repeat.

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_aff01e4d339bda474a66984b709044b63}{mouse\+Drag}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_desktop_a484c8460c95255150aef4dbe1909ae9f}{Desktop\+::begin\+Drag\+Auto\+Repeat}} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{class_component_a4bf084bcf5b0e4398ee3a0007f803865}\label{class_component_a4bf084bcf5b0e4398ee3a0007f803865}}

The component may have been brought to the front by the \mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_a511e6baefd7455d0163480fe858e733c}{to\+Front()}} method, or by the operating system if it\textquotesingle{}s a top-\/level window.

\mbox{\Hypertarget{class_component_abec1d60cfacf16eab602dff06932fbca}\label{class_component_abec1d60cfacf16eab602dff06932fbca}} 
\index{Component@{Component}!canModalEventBeSentToComponent@{canModalEventBeSentToComponent}}
\index{canModalEventBeSentToComponent@{canModalEventBeSentToComponent}!Component@{Component}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{canModalEventBeSentToComponent()}{canModalEventBeSentToComponent()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily virtual bool Component\+::can\+Modal\+Event\+Be\+Sent\+To\+Component (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{zconf_8in_8h_a2c212835823e3c54a8ab6d95c652660e}{const}} \mbox{\hyperlink{class_component}{Component}} $\ast$}]{target\+Component }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [virtual]}}

When a component is modal, this callback allows it to choose which other components can still receive events.

When a modal component is active and the user clicks on a non-\/modal component, this method is called on the modal component, and if it returns true, the event is allowed to reach its target. If it returns false, the event is blocked and the \mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_a260e46fb72d4b3210bc46a658a21fbb5}{input\+Attempt\+When\+Modal()}} callback is made.

It called by the \mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_a70fc33489ec892d615452dfdbd4687db}{is\+Currently\+Blocked\+By\+Another\+Modal\+Component()}} method. The default implementation just returns false in all cases. 

Reimplemented in \mbox{\hyperlink{classjuce_1_1_toolbar_1_1_customisation_dialog_a91d50ef68b6655caff17d5a9613362aa}{juce\+::\+Toolbar\+::\+Customisation\+Dialog}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{classjuce_1_1_drag_and_drop_container_1_1_drag_image_component_a97b90869475a18e8f9b8d4389ff3f589}{juce\+::\+Drag\+And\+Drop\+Container\+::\+Drag\+Image\+Component}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{classjuce_1_1_file_chooser_1_1_native_aa3aff359891039a46dc52e6acecbe524}{juce\+::\+File\+Chooser\+::\+Native}}, and \mbox{\hyperlink{classjuce_1_1_file_chooser_1_1_native_aa3aff359891039a46dc52e6acecbe524}{juce\+::\+File\+Chooser\+::\+Native}}.

\index{contains@{contains}!Component@{Component}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{contains()}{contains()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [2/3]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily bool Component\+::contains (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{class_point}{Point}}$<$ float $>$}]{local\+Point }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Returns true if a given point lies within this component or one of its children.

Never override this method! Use hit\+Test to create custom hit regions.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em local\+Point} & the coordinate to test, relative to this component\textquotesingle{}s top-\/left. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
true if the point is within the component\textquotesingle{}s hit-\/test area, but only if that part of the component isn\textquotesingle{}t clipped by its parent component. Note that this won\textquotesingle{}t take into account any overlapping sibling components which might be in the way -\/ for that, see \mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_aa8d8eb035156e46e6264f600097b1cc1}{really\+Contains()}} 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}

\end{DoxySeeAlso}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{copyAllExplicitColoursTo()}{copyAllExplicitColoursTo()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{png_8h_aa8c59027f9ab2769342f248709d68d17}{void}} Component\+::copy\+All\+Explicit\+Colours\+To (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{class_component}{Component}} \&}]{target }\end{DoxyParamCaption}) const}

This looks for any colours that have been specified for this component, and copies them to the specified target component. \mbox{\Hypertarget{class_component_a275e46e5a8147f89c142c91ba5c793a5}\label{class_component_a275e46e5a8147f89c142c91ba5c793a5}} 
\index{Component@{Component}!createComponentSnapshot@{createComponentSnapshot}}
\index{createComponentSnapshot@{createComponentSnapshot}!Component@{Component}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{createComponentSnapshot()}{createComponentSnapshot()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{class_image}{Image}} Component\+::create\+Component\+Snapshot (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{class_rectangle}{Rectangle}}$<$ \mbox{\hyperlink{group__juce__audio__plugin__client-_unity_ga966b05a42d98c7296097e073c627dcd0}{int}} $>$}]{area\+To\+Grab,  }\item[{bool}]{clip\+Image\+To\+Component\+Bounds = {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{ordinals_8h_a41f9c5fb8b08eb5dc3edce4dcb37fee7}{true}}},  }\item[{float}]{scale\+Factor = {\ttfamily 1.0f} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Generates a snapshot of part of this component.

This will return a new \mbox{\hyperlink{class_image}{Image}}, the size of the rectangle specified, containing a snapshot of the specified area of the component and all its children.

The image may or may not have an alpha-\/channel, depending on whether the image is opaque or not.

If the clip\+Image\+To\+Component\+Bounds parameter is true and the area is greater than the size of the component, it\textquotesingle{}ll be clipped. If clip\+Image\+To\+Component\+Bounds is false then parts of the component beyond its bounds can be drawn.

\end{DoxySeeAlso}

\index{Component@{Component}!createFocusTraverser@{createFocusTraverser}}
\index{createFocusTraverser@{createFocusTraverser}!Component@{Component}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{createFocusTraverser()}{createFocusTraverser()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily virtual std\+::unique\+\_\+ptr$<$ \mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_traverser}{Component\+Traverser}} $>$ Component\+::create\+Focus\+Traverser (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [virtual]}}

Creates a \mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_traverser}{Component\+Traverser}} object to determine the logic by which focus should be passed from this component.

The default implementation of this method will return an instance of \mbox{\hyperlink{class_focus_traverser}{Focus\+Traverser}} if this component is a focus container (as determined by the \mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_a5c6ce0b41244e147db85274cbac0e84d}{set\+Focus\+Container\+Type()}} method). If the component isn\textquotesingle{}t a focus container, then it will recursively call \mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_a138dc2e3c7f4836d7c127409dab8a56d}{create\+Focus\+Traverser()}} on its parents.

If you override this to return a custom traverser object, then this component and all its sub-\/components will use the new object to make their focusing decisions. \mbox{\Hypertarget{class_component_a0a2c598d8ebdfcd1bea0de47fae422e3}\label{class_component_a0a2c598d8ebdfcd1bea0de47fae422e3}} 
\index{Component@{Component}!createIgnoredAccessibilityHandler@{createIgnoredAccessibilityHandler}}
\index{createIgnoredAccessibilityHandler@{createIgnoredAccessibilityHandler}!Component@{Component}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{createIgnoredAccessibilityHandler()}{createIgnoredAccessibilityHandler()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily static std\+::unique\+\_\+ptr$<$ \mbox{\hyperlink{class_accessibility_handler}{Accessibility\+Handler}} $>$ Component\+::create\+Ignored\+Accessibility\+Handler (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{class_component}{Component}} \&}]{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [static]}, {\ttfamily [protected]}}

\mbox{\Hypertarget{class_component_a8dc872ef83fedecd89cf814d28236cd0}\label{class_component_a8dc872ef83fedecd89cf814d28236cd0}} 
\index{Component@{Component}!createKeyboardFocusTraverser@{createKeyboardFocusTraverser}}
\index{createKeyboardFocusTraverser@{createKeyboardFocusTraverser}!Component@{Component}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{createKeyboardFocusTraverser()}{createKeyboardFocusTraverser()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily virtual std\+::unique\+\_\+ptr$<$ \mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_traverser}{Component\+Traverser}} $>$ Component\+::create\+Keyboard\+Focus\+Traverser (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [virtual]}}

Creates a \mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_traverser}{Component\+Traverser}} object to use to determine the logic by which keyboard focus should be passed from this component.

The default implementation of this method will return an instance of \mbox{\hyperlink{class_keyboard_focus_traverser}{Keyboard\+Focus\+Traverser}} if this component is a keyboard focus container (as determined by the \mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_a5c6ce0b41244e147db85274cbac0e84d}{set\+Focus\+Container\+Type()}} method). If the component isn\textquotesingle{}t a keyboard focus container, then it will recursively call \mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_a8dc872ef83fedecd89cf814d28236cd0}{create\+Keyboard\+Focus\+Traverser()}} on its parents.

If you override this to return a custom traverser object, then this component and all its sub-\/components will use the new object to make their keyboard focusing decisions. 

Reimplemented in \mbox{\hyperlink{class_filename_component_a9fdf2cae4ebaba95dafd2939c57b4273}{Filename\+Component}}, and \mbox{\hyperlink{class_label_a1dc56d219635f3dd8249681b9e0482a5}{Label}}.

\mbox{\Hypertarget{class_component_abc8f8338a400c20d5e941ea3a1f67f7b}\label{class_component_abc8f8338a400c20d5e941ea3a1f67f7b}} 
\index{Component@{Component}!deleteAllChildren@{deleteAllChildren}}
\index{deleteAllChildren@{deleteAllChildren}!Component@{Component}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{deleteAllChildren()}{deleteAllChildren()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{png_8h_aa8c59027f9ab2769342f248709d68d17}{void}} Component\+::delete\+All\+Children (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Removes and deletes all of this component\textquotesingle{}s children. My advice is to avoid this method! It\textquotesingle{}s an old function that is only kept here for backwards-\/compatibility with legacy code, and should be viewed with extreme suspicion by anyone attempting to write modern C++. In almost all cases, it\textquotesingle{}s much smarter to manage the lifetimes of your child components via modern RAII techniques such as simply making them member variables, or using std\+::unique\+\_\+ptr, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_owned_array}{Owned\+Array}}, etc to manage their lifetimes appropriately. \begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_a72ee4d44ce3b3954e8a00e5225201b6d}{remove\+All\+Children}} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{class_component_a8e5e39d3d7e2b8be4e78454ec4a5f584}\label{class_component_a8e5e39d3d7e2b8be4e78454ec4a5f584}} 
\index{Component@{Component}!enablementChanged@{enablementChanged}}
\index{enablementChanged@{enablementChanged}!Component@{Component}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{enablementChanged()}{enablementChanged()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily virtual \mbox{\hyperlink{png_8h_aa8c59027f9ab2769342f248709d68d17}{void}} Component\+::enablement\+Changed (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [virtual]}}

Callback to indicate that this component has been enabled or disabled.

This can be triggered by one of the component\textquotesingle{}s parent components being enabled or disabled, as well as changes to the component itself.

The default implementation of this method does nothing; your class may wish to repaint itself or something when this happens.

\end{DoxySeeAlso}


Reimplemented in \mbox{\hyperlink{class_button_aacc3dbdf54be71a697272d2821b86d84}{Button}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_drawable_button_a726b866e69adc70a147a2c59156da249}{Drawable\+Button}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_toolbar_button_a3308004ba6d256b066a42cc510335d13}{Toolbar\+Button}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_group_component_a41a11e08ba69af80e571e84c084feba7}{Group\+Component}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{classjuce_1_1_tabbed_button_bar_1_1_behind_front_tab_comp_a4c40da2a94208a94b3b958c834462403}{juce\+::\+Tabbed\+Button\+Bar\+::\+Behind\+Front\+Tab\+Comp}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_property_component_a5b75f072da6b54155076ddc5c5cf22da}{Property\+Component}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_combo_box_adeabe2c0edc2170647ba741a8938aa2c}{Combo\+Box}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_label_ad6c81f949fd72d2382ffcd336f1a5923}{Label}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_slider_a5d5dddfd7d8f254d9097724493878cc1}{Slider}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_text_editor_ae323b4ceb59be7c1e8a1f9a637193267}{Text\+Editor}}, and \mbox{\hyperlink{class_tree_view_a25ee8644a3b0d300f33178c87d13fcfa}{Tree\+View}}.

\mbox{\Hypertarget{class_component_a0e7be8c456a663615eb389ecd10b2c04}\label{class_component_a0e7be8c456a663615eb389ecd10b2c04}} 
\index{Component@{Component}!enterModalState@{enterModalState}}
\index{enterModalState@{enterModalState}!Component@{Component}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{enterModalState()}{enterModalState()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{png_8h_aa8c59027f9ab2769342f248709d68d17}{void}} Component\+::enter\+Modal\+State (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{bool}]{take\+Keyboard\+Focus = {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{ordinals_8h_a41f9c5fb8b08eb5dc3edce4dcb37fee7}{true}}},  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{class_modal_component_manager_1_1_callback}{Modal\+Component\+Manager\+::\+Callback}} $\ast$}]{callback = {\ttfamily nullptr},  }\item[{bool}]{delete\+When\+Dismissed = {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{ordinals_8h_a65e9886d74aaee76545e83dd09011727}{false}}} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Puts the component into a modal state.

This makes the component modal, so that messages are blocked from reaching any components other than this one and its children, but unlike run\+Modal\+Loop(), this method returns immediately.

If take\+Keyboard\+Focus is true, the component will use \mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_a91886a0e276d27719fa8866a95306571}{grab\+Keyboard\+Focus()}} to get the focus, which is usually what you\textquotesingle{}ll want it to do. If not, it will leave the focus unchanged.

The callback is an optional object which will receive a callback when the modal component loses its modal status, either by being hidden or when \mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_a686e2440370ff4a97c7a7851907be650}{exit\+Modal\+State()}} is called. If you pass an object in here, the system will take care of deleting it later, after making the callback

If delete\+When\+Dismissed is true, then when it is dismissed, the component will be deleted and then the callback will be called. (This will safely handle the situation where the component is deleted before its \mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_a686e2440370ff4a97c7a7851907be650}{exit\+Modal\+State()}} method is called).

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_a686e2440370ff4a97c7a7851907be650}{exit\+Modal\+State}}, run\+Modal\+Loop, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_modal_component_manager_a2ce962253cf2c8e42d5575ad2a41d888}{Modal\+Component\+Manager\+::attach\+Callback}} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{class_component_a686e2440370ff4a97c7a7851907be650}\label{class_component_a686e2440370ff4a97c7a7851907be650}} 
\index{Component@{Component}!exitModalState@{exitModalState}}
\index{exitModalState@{exitModalState}!Component@{Component}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{exitModalState()}{exitModalState()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{png_8h_aa8c59027f9ab2769342f248709d68d17}{void}} Component\+::exit\+Modal\+State (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group__juce__audio__plugin__client-_unity_ga966b05a42d98c7296097e073c627dcd0}{int}}}]{return\+Value }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Ends a component\textquotesingle{}s modal state.

If this component is currently modal, this will turn off its modalness, and return a value to the run\+Modal\+Loop() method that might have be running its modal loop.

\end{DoxySeeAlso}

\index{Component@{Component}!findColour@{findColour}}
\index{findColour@{findColour}!Component@{Component}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{findColour()}{findColour()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{class_colour}{Colour}} Component\+::find\+Colour (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group__juce__audio__plugin__client-_unity_ga966b05a42d98c7296097e073c627dcd0}{int}}}]{colour\+ID,  }\item[{bool}]{inherit\+From\+Parent = {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{ordinals_8h_a65e9886d74aaee76545e83dd09011727}{false}}} }\end{DoxyParamCaption}) const}

Looks for a colour that has been registered with the given colour ID number.

If a colour has been set for this ID number using \mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_aad68f45fb458d0cac645c0910193142d}{set\+Colour()}}, then it is returned. If none has been set, the method will try calling the component\textquotesingle{}s \mbox{\hyperlink{class_look_and_feel}{Look\+And\+Feel}} class\textquotesingle{}s \mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_a743504b7a85b697404bf9aab17324265}{find\+Colour()}} method. If none has been registered with the look-\/and-\/feel either, it will just return black.

The colour IDs for various purposes are stored as enums in the components that they are relevant to -\/ for an example, see \mbox{\hyperlink{class_slider_a1012002c53381ccc7c1fe7e604a75f44}{Slider\+::\+Colour\+Ids}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_label_a41756012394513222e1323bb432fa701}{Label\+::\+Colour\+Ids}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_text_editor_aa805220923c93cd808a92fff0e3fb71d}{Text\+Editor\+::\+Colour\+Ids}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_tree_view_abeebe6dbdc6ae466495aabc64eb51d6a}{Tree\+View\+::\+Colour\+Ids}}, etc.

\end{DoxySeeAlso}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily template$<$class Target\+Class $>$ \\
Target\+Class $\ast$ Component\+::find\+Parent\+Component\+Of\+Class (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption}) const\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}

Searches the parent components for a component of a specified class.

For example find\+Parent\+Component\+Of\+Class \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}My\+Comp\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}() would return the first parent component that can be dynamically cast to a My\+Comp, or will return nullptr if none of the parents are suitable. \mbox{\Hypertarget{class_component_a408d41f1499a2ebdd4bbc8d4004c7727}\label{class_component_a408d41f1499a2ebdd4bbc8d4004c7727}}

\index{Component@{Component}!focusOfChildComponentChanged@{focusOfChildComponentChanged}}
\index{focusOfChildComponentChanged@{focusOfChildComponentChanged}!Component@{Component}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{focusOfChildComponentChanged()}{focusOfChildComponentChanged()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily virtual \mbox{\hyperlink{png_8h_aa8c59027f9ab2769342f248709d68d17}{void}} Component\+::focus\+Of\+Child\+Component\+Changed (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_a7fd775ea6b1190d5d694fdffa539dfac}{Focus\+Change\+Type}}}]{cause }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [virtual]}}

Called to indicate a change in whether or not this component is the parent of the currently-\/focused component.

Essentially this is called when the return value of a call to has\+Keyboard\+Focus (true) has changed. It happens when focus moves from one of this component\textquotesingle{}s children (at any depth) to a component that isn\textquotesingle{}t contained in this one, (or vice-\/versa). Note that this method does NOT get called to when focus simply moves from one of its child components to another.

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_a408d41f1499a2ebdd4bbc8d4004c7727}{focus\+Gained}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_a6a1f21a76b971d54870cb5c32c041055}{set\+Wants\+Keyboard\+Focus}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_aa056639955cf136ee527e1a7425887b8}{get\+Currently\+Focused\+Component}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_abf76cf5c3550c5c83bc585f86429b397}{has\+Keyboard\+Focus}} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{group__juce__audio__plugin__client-_unity_ga966b05a42d98c7296097e073c627dcd0}{int}} Component\+::get\+Bottom (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption}) const\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}, {\ttfamily [noexcept]}}

Returns the y coordinate of the bottom edge of this component. This is a distance in pixels from the top edge of the component\textquotesingle{}s parent.

Note that if you\textquotesingle{}ve used \mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_a42d13229962acb1cdf4328c4a490ffef}{set\+Transform()}} to apply a transform, then the component\textquotesingle{}s bounds will no longer be a direct reflection of the position at which it appears within its parent, as the transform will be applied to its bounding box. \mbox{\Hypertarget{class_component_aefedbd2b157e26f7af2502d8648a11ef}\label{class_component_aefedbd2b157e26f7af2502d8648a11ef}}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{getBounds()}{getBounds()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{class_rectangle}{Rectangle}}$<$ \mbox{\hyperlink{group__juce__audio__plugin__client-_unity_ga966b05a42d98c7296097e073c627dcd0}{int}} $>$ Component\+::get\+Bounds (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption}) const\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}, {\ttfamily [noexcept]}}

Returns this component\textquotesingle{}s bounding box. The rectangle returned is relative to the top-\/left of the component\textquotesingle{}s parent.

Note that if you\textquotesingle{}ve used \mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_a42d13229962acb1cdf4328c4a490ffef}{set\+Transform()}} to apply a transform, then the component\textquotesingle{}s bounds will no longer be a direct reflection of the position at which it appears within its parent, as the transform will be applied to its bounding box. \mbox{\Hypertarget{class_component_ad9e70e7f3bc3c1e2287423941acb866f}\label{class_component_ad9e70e7f3bc3c1e2287423941acb866f}} 
\index{Component@{Component}!getBoundsInParent@{getBoundsInParent}}
\index{getBoundsInParent@{getBoundsInParent}!Component@{Component}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{getBoundsInParent()}{getBoundsInParent()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{class_rectangle}{Rectangle}}$<$ \mbox{\hyperlink{group__juce__audio__plugin__client-_unity_ga966b05a42d98c7296097e073c627dcd0}{int}} $>$ Component\+::get\+Bounds\+In\+Parent (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption}) const\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [noexcept]}}

Returns the area of this component\textquotesingle{}s parent which this component covers.

The returned area is relative to the parent\textquotesingle{}s coordinate space. If the component has an affine transform specified, then the resulting area will be the smallest rectangle that fully covers the component\textquotesingle{}s transformed bounding box. If this component has no parent, the return value will simply be the same as \mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_aefedbd2b157e26f7af2502d8648a11ef}{get\+Bounds()}}. \mbox{\Hypertarget{class_component_a31c2f31197c3f29c55eb0b35c8e7c1ce}\label{class_component_a31c2f31197c3f29c55eb0b35c8e7c1ce}}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{class_component}{Component}} $\ast$ Component\+::get\+Child\+Component (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group__juce__audio__plugin__client-_unity_ga966b05a42d98c7296097e073c627dcd0}{int}}}]{index }\end{DoxyParamCaption}) const\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [noexcept]}}

Returns one of this component\textquotesingle{}s child components, by it index.

The component with index 0 is at the back of the z-\/order, the one at the front will have index (\mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_afa33580cab86ac3b80c9c1f9d85ad81d}{get\+Num\+Child\+Components()}} -\/ 1).

If the index is out-\/of-\/range, this will return a null pointer.

{\footnotesize\ttfamily static \mbox{\hyperlink{class_component}{Component}} $\ast$\mbox{\hyperlink{group__juce__core-system_gaf0b3f78ca801d88a7912f4c6bbf50e58}{JUCE\+\_\+\+CALLTYPE}} Component\+::get\+Currently\+Focused\+Component (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [static]}, {\ttfamily [noexcept]}}

Returns the component that currently has the keyboard focus.

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}

\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{class_component_a0a626d27dd0b706c869ea9a60f777ee6}\label{class_component_a0a626d27dd0b706c869ea9a60f777ee6}} 
\index{Component@{Component}!getCurrentlyModalComponent@{getCurrentlyModalComponent}}
\index{getCurrentlyModalComponent@{getCurrentlyModalComponent}!Component@{Component}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{getCurrentlyModalComponent()}{getCurrentlyModalComponent()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily static \mbox{\hyperlink{class_component}{Component}} $\ast$\mbox{\hyperlink{group__juce__core-system_gaf0b3f78ca801d88a7912f4c6bbf50e58}{JUCE\+\_\+\+CALLTYPE}} Component\+::get\+Currently\+Modal\+Component (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group__juce__audio__plugin__client-_unity_ga966b05a42d98c7296097e073c627dcd0}{int}}}]{index = {\ttfamily 0} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [static]}, {\ttfamily [noexcept]}}

Returns one of the components that are currently modal.

The index specifies which of the possible modal components to return. The order of the components in this list is the reverse of the order in which they became modal -\/ so the component at index 0 is always the active component, and the others are progressively earlier ones that are themselves now blocked by later ones.

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
the modal component, or null if no components are modal (or if the index is out of range) 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_ae58129a62eda13ca8987072cd9c62359}{get\+Num\+Currently\+Modal\+Components}}, run\+Modal\+Loop, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_a489ebde1970d6a2571bae5152b396267}{is\+Currently\+Modal}} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}

\index{Component@{Component}!getDesktopScaleFactor@{getDesktopScaleFactor}}
\index{getDesktopScaleFactor@{getDesktopScaleFactor}!Component@{Component}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{getDesktopScaleFactor()}{getDesktopScaleFactor()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily virtual float Component\+::get\+Desktop\+Scale\+Factor (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption}) const\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [virtual]}}

Returns the default scale factor to use for this component when it is placed on the desktop. The default implementation of this method just returns the value from \mbox{\hyperlink{class_desktop_a9d3762d46b652cd0249e6845229f3b4c}{Desktop\+::get\+Global\+Scale\+Factor()}}, but it can be overridden if a particular component has different requirements. The method only used if this component is added to the desktop -\/ it has no effect for child components. 

Reimplemented in \mbox{\hyperlink{structjuce_1_1_popup_menu_1_1_helper_classes_1_1_menu_window_a6adb6de3057b8d31ba2061488ec6233b}{juce\+::\+Popup\+Menu\+::\+Helper\+Classes\+::\+Menu\+Window}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{classjuce_1_1_drop_shadower_1_1_shadow_window_a0750117bf3b627de99ac1f9e8a62ccc2}{juce\+::\+Drop\+Shadower\+::\+Shadow\+Window}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{structjuce_1_1_outline_window_component_a529a170d6d43bfd17b94cf264b5b22a8}{juce\+::\+Outline\+Window\+Component}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_alert_window_a6921c5f182147f036232278babccabfb}{Alert\+Window}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_dialog_window_af7d853cf3eb4c0bae2bb6ccf77b0d038}{Dialog\+Window}}, and \mbox{\hyperlink{class_tooltip_window_a5aa4b08bea58ede7297bd6e87b3fbd26}{Tooltip\+Window}}.

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{getIndexOfChildComponent()}{getIndexOfChildComponent()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{group__juce__audio__plugin__client-_unity_ga966b05a42d98c7296097e073c627dcd0}{int}} Component\+::get\+Index\+Of\+Child\+Component (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{zconf_8in_8h_a2c212835823e3c54a8ab6d95c652660e}{const}} \mbox{\hyperlink{class_component}{Component}} $\ast$}]{child }\end{DoxyParamCaption}) const\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [noexcept]}}

Returns the index of this component in the list of child components.

A value of 0 means it is first in the list (i.\+e. behind all other components). Higher values are further towards the front.

Returns -\/1 if the component passed-\/in is not a child of this component.

\index{Component@{Component}!getLocalArea@{getLocalArea}}
\index{getLocalArea@{getLocalArea}!Component@{Component}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{getLocalArea()}{getLocalArea()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{class_rectangle}{Rectangle}}$<$ float $>$ Component\+::get\+Local\+Area (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{zconf_8in_8h_a2c212835823e3c54a8ab6d95c652660e}{const}} \mbox{\hyperlink{class_component}{Component}} $\ast$}]{source\+Component,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{class_rectangle}{Rectangle}}$<$ float $>$}]{area\+Relative\+To\+Source\+Component }\end{DoxyParamCaption}) const}

Converts a rectangle to be relative to this component\textquotesingle{}s coordinate space.

This takes a rectangle that is relative to a different component, and returns its position relative to this component. If the source\+Component parameter is null, the source rectangle is assumed to be a screen coordinate.

If you\textquotesingle{}ve used \mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_a42d13229962acb1cdf4328c4a490ffef}{set\+Transform()}} to apply one or more transforms to components, then the source rectangle may not actually be rectangular when converted to the target space, so in that situation this will return the smallest rectangle that fully contains the transformed area. \mbox{\Hypertarget{class_component_aca4c6cfd387cd130308bb953def4b7d0}\label{class_component_aca4c6cfd387cd130308bb953def4b7d0}} 
\index{Component@{Component}!getLocalArea@{getLocalArea}}
\index{getLocalArea@{getLocalArea}!Component@{Component}}

Converts a rectangle to be relative to this component\textquotesingle{}s coordinate space.

This takes a rectangle that is relative to a different component, and returns its position relative to this component. If the source\+Component parameter is null, the source rectangle is assumed to be a screen coordinate.

If you\textquotesingle{}ve used \mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_a42d13229962acb1cdf4328c4a490ffef}{set\+Transform()}} to apply one or more transforms to components, then the source rectangle may not actually be rectangular when converted to the target space, so in that situation this will return the smallest rectangle that fully contains the transformed area. \mbox{\Hypertarget{class_component_a0bb195a619802a5e8d4ed2218394816f}\label{class_component_a0bb195a619802a5e8d4ed2218394816f}}

\index{getPeer@{getPeer}!Component@{Component}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{getPeer()}{getPeer()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_peer}{Component\+Peer}} $\ast$ Component\+::get\+Peer (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption}) const}

Returns the heavyweight window that contains this component.

If this component is itself on the desktop, this will return the window object that it is using. Otherwise, it will return the window of its top-\/level parent component.

This may return nullptr if there isn\textquotesingle{}t a desktop component.

\index{Component@{Component}!giveAwayKeyboardFocus@{giveAwayKeyboardFocus}}
\index{giveAwayKeyboardFocus@{giveAwayKeyboardFocus}!Component@{Component}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{giveAwayKeyboardFocus()}{giveAwayKeyboardFocus()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{png_8h_aa8c59027f9ab2769342f248709d68d17}{void}} Component\+::give\+Away\+Keyboard\+Focus (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

If this component or any of its children currently have the keyboard focus, this will defocus it, send a focus change notification, and try to pass the focus to the next component.

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_a91886a0e276d27719fa8866a95306571}{grab\+Keyboard\+Focus}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_a6a1f21a76b971d54870cb5c32c041055}{set\+Wants\+Keyboard\+Focus}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_aa056639955cf136ee527e1a7425887b8}{get\+Currently\+Focused\+Component}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_a408d41f1499a2ebdd4bbc8d4004c7727}{focus\+Gained}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_a36456ea9d5a14172d6e96527ec1f59c8}{focus\+Lost}} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{class_component_a91886a0e276d27719fa8866a95306571}\label{class_component_a91886a0e276d27719fa8866a95306571}} 
\index{Component@{Component}!grabKeyboardFocus@{grabKeyboardFocus}}
\index{grabKeyboardFocus@{grabKeyboardFocus}!Component@{Component}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{grabKeyboardFocus()}{grabKeyboardFocus()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{png_8h_aa8c59027f9ab2769342f248709d68d17}{void}} Component\+::grab\+Keyboard\+Focus (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Tries to give keyboard focus to this component.

When the user clicks on a component or its \mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_a91886a0e276d27719fa8866a95306571}{grab\+Keyboard\+Focus()}} method is called, the following procedure is used to work out which component should get it\+:


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item if the component that was clicked on actually wants focus (as indicated by calling get\+Wants\+Keyboard\+Focus), it gets it.
\item if the component itself doesn\textquotesingle{}t want focus, it will try to pass it on to whichever of its children is the default component, as determined by the get\+Default\+Component() implementation of the \mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_traverser}{Component\+Traverser}} returned by \mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_a8dc872ef83fedecd89cf814d28236cd0}{create\+Keyboard\+Focus\+Traverser()}}.
\item if none of its children want focus at all, it will pass it up to its parent instead, unless it\textquotesingle{}s a top-\/level component without a parent, in which case it just takes the focus itself.
\end{DoxyItemize}

Important note! It\textquotesingle{}s obviously not possible for a component to be focused unless it\textquotesingle{}s actually visible, on-\/screen, and inside a window that is also visible. So there\textquotesingle{}s no point trying to call this in the component\textquotesingle{}s own constructor or before all of its parent hierarchy has been fully instantiated.

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_a0492ed11cb7fb9102b8284bccb0d9d78}{give\+Away\+Keyboard\+Focus}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_a6a1f21a76b971d54870cb5c32c041055}{set\+Wants\+Keyboard\+Focus}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_af3618b8c0d0583705db9918f23784833}{get\+Wants\+Keyboard\+Focus}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_abf76cf5c3550c5c83bc585f86429b397}{has\+Keyboard\+Focus}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_aa056639955cf136ee527e1a7425887b8}{get\+Currently\+Focused\+Component}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_a408d41f1499a2ebdd4bbc8d4004c7727}{focus\+Gained}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_a36456ea9d5a14172d6e96527ec1f59c8}{focus\+Lost}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_ab063a5c631854864da09106abec78a86}{key\+Pressed}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_aeff4d2fdbae4d5974e43b62ab3c304f9}{key\+State\+Changed}} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{class_component_a9ba6fa31d1397c7e90050b2cd4f2089b}\label{class_component_a9ba6fa31d1397c7e90050b2cd4f2089b}}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily virtual \mbox{\hyperlink{png_8h_aa8c59027f9ab2769342f248709d68d17}{void}} Component\+::handle\+Command\+Message (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group__juce__audio__plugin__client-_unity_ga966b05a42d98c7296097e073c627dcd0}{int}}}]{command\+Id }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [virtual]}}

This is called by the message thread when a command message arrives, and the component can override this method to process it in any way it needs to.

Returns true if this component currently has the keyboard focus.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em true\+If\+Child\+Is\+Focused} & if this is true, then the method returns true if either this component or any of its children (recursively) have the focus. If false, the method only returns true if this component has the focus.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_a91886a0e276d27719fa8866a95306571}{grab\+Keyboard\+Focus}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_a0492ed11cb7fb9102b8284bccb0d9d78}{give\+Away\+Keyboard\+Focus}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_a6a1f21a76b971d54870cb5c32c041055}{set\+Wants\+Keyboard\+Focus}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_aa056639955cf136ee527e1a7425887b8}{get\+Currently\+Focused\+Component}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_a408d41f1499a2ebdd4bbc8d4004c7727}{focus\+Gained}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_a36456ea9d5a14172d6e96527ec1f59c8}{focus\+Lost}} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{class_component_a2da9631236e1cbf1b340454209a6c9e0}\label{class_component_a2da9631236e1cbf1b340454209a6c9e0}} 
\index{Component@{Component}!hitTest@{hitTest}}
\index{hitTest@{hitTest}!Component@{Component}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{hitTest()}{hitTest()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily virtual bool Component\+::hit\+Test (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group__juce__audio__plugin__client-_unity_ga966b05a42d98c7296097e073c627dcd0}{int}}}]{x,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group__juce__audio__plugin__client-_unity_ga966b05a42d98c7296097e073c627dcd0}{int}}}]{y }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [virtual]}}

Tests whether a given point is inside the component.

Overriding this method allows you to create components which only intercept mouse-\/clicks within a user-\/defined area.

This is called to find out whether a particular x, y coordinate is considered to be inside the component or not, and is used by methods such as \mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_a6b697f6caaa753756251b4eb5ece302b}{contains()}} and \mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_a054f5a6add8f7dd6ce7cd088bc5e579f}{get\+Component\+At()}} to work out which component the mouse is clicked on.

Components with custom shapes will probably want to override it to perform some more complex hit-\/testing.

The default implementation of this method returns either true or false, depending on the value that was set by calling \mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_ac9fdcb595c1878201a641de2e1159aec}{set\+Intercepts\+Mouse\+Clicks()}} (true is the default return value).

Note that the hit-\/test region is not related to the opacity with which areas of a component are painted.

Applications should never call \mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_a2da9631236e1cbf1b340454209a6c9e0}{hit\+Test()}} directly -\/ instead use the \mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_a6b697f6caaa753756251b4eb5ece302b}{contains()}} method, because this will also test for occlusion by the component\textquotesingle{}s parent.

Note that for components on the desktop, this method will be ignored, because it\textquotesingle{}s not always possible to implement this behaviour on all platforms.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em x} & the x coordinate to test, relative to the left hand edge of this component. This value is guaranteed to be greater than or equal to zero, and less than the component\textquotesingle{}s width \\
\hline
{\em y} & the y coordinate to test, relative to the top edge of this component. This value is guaranteed to be greater than or equal to zero, and less than the component\textquotesingle{}s height \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
true if the click is considered to be inside the component 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_ac9fdcb595c1878201a641de2e1159aec}{set\+Intercepts\+Mouse\+Clicks}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_a6b697f6caaa753756251b4eb5ece302b}{contains}} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}


Reimplemented in \mbox{\hyperlink{class_image_button_a646b175c55ac588b8ffed117f213e8e2}{Image\+Button}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_drawable_image_a0a6bd602f7d8dd85366b11b7419209ed}{Drawable\+Image}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_drawable_shape_ab5862ed42c7976a43791f56ae6173c27}{Drawable\+Shape}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_resizable_border_component_acd797e21238848968eb9957106590253}{Resizable\+Border\+Component}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_resizable_corner_component_acc3a046566ad8ab5aa5318b3a943d2fc}{Resizable\+Corner\+Component}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_tab_bar_button_ac6e24e3e9b5001e36a3014692257ea03}{Tab\+Bar\+Button}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_call_out_box_a916cce375fb38ac4e77e4a8ef27591b6}{Call\+Out\+Box}}, and \mbox{\hyperlink{class_lasso_component_ab67925a4436687bc41437c8460de710d}{Lasso\+Component$<$ Selectable\+Item\+Type $>$}}.

\mbox{\Hypertarget{class_component_a260e46fb72d4b3210bc46a658a21fbb5}\label{class_component_a260e46fb72d4b3210bc46a658a21fbb5}} 
\index{Component@{Component}!inputAttemptWhenModal@{inputAttemptWhenModal}}
\index{inputAttemptWhenModal@{inputAttemptWhenModal}!Component@{Component}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{inputAttemptWhenModal()}{inputAttemptWhenModal()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily virtual \mbox{\hyperlink{png_8h_aa8c59027f9ab2769342f248709d68d17}{void}} Component\+::input\+Attempt\+When\+Modal (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [virtual]}}

Called when the user tries to click on a component that is blocked by another modal component.

When a component is modal and the user clicks on one of the other components, the modal component will receive this callback.

The default implementation of this method will play a beep, and bring the currently modal component to the front, but it can be overridden to do other tasks.

{\footnotesize\ttfamily bool Component\+::is\+Currently\+Blocked\+By\+Another\+Modal\+Component (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption}) const}

Checks whether there\textquotesingle{}s a modal component somewhere that\textquotesingle{}s stopping this one from receiving messages.

If there is a modal component, its \mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_abec1d60cfacf16eab602dff06932fbca}{can\+Modal\+Event\+Be\+Sent\+To\+Component()}} method will be called to see if it will still allow this component to receive events.

\mbox{\Hypertarget{class_component_a489ebde1970d6a2571bae5152b396267}\label{class_component_a489ebde1970d6a2571bae5152b396267}} 
\index{Component@{Component}!isCurrentlyModal@{isCurrentlyModal}}
\index{isCurrentlyModal@{isCurrentlyModal}!Component@{Component}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{isCurrentlyModal()}{isCurrentlyModal()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily bool Component\+::is\+Currently\+Modal (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{bool}]{only\+Consider\+Foremost\+Modal\+Component = {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{ordinals_8h_a41f9c5fb8b08eb5dc3edce4dcb37fee7}{true}}} }\end{DoxyParamCaption}) const\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [noexcept]}}

Returns true if this component is the modal one.

It\textquotesingle{}s possible to have nested modal components, e.\+g. a pop-\/up dialog box that launches another pop-\/up. If only\+Consider\+Foremost\+Modal\+Component is true then is\+Currently\+Modal will only return true for the one at the top of the stack. If only\+Consider\+Foremost\+Modal\+Component is false then is\+Currently\+Modal will return true for any modal component in the stack.

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_a0a626d27dd0b706c869ea9a60f777ee6}{get\+Currently\+Modal\+Component}} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{class_component_a0e12726e34fdd284f036922597914bb3}\label{class_component_a0e12726e34fdd284f036922597914bb3}} 
\index{Component@{Component}!isEnabled@{isEnabled}}
\index{isEnabled@{isEnabled}!Component@{Component}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{isEnabled()}{isEnabled()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily bool Component\+::is\+Enabled (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption}) const\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [noexcept]}}

Returns true if the component (and all its parents) are enabled.

Components are enabled by default, and can be disabled with \mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_a6f956f690d72256838146c7dfe99bc0e}{set\+Enabled()}}. Exactly what difference this makes to the component depends on the type. E.\+g. buttons and sliders will choose to draw themselves differently, etc.

Note that if one of this component\textquotesingle{}s parents is disabled, this will always return false, even if this component itself is enabled.

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_a6f956f690d72256838146c7dfe99bc0e}{set\+Enabled}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_a8e5e39d3d7e2b8be4e78454ec4a5f584}{enablement\+Changed}} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{isMouseButtonDown()}{isMouseButtonDown()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily bool Component\+::is\+Mouse\+Button\+Down (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{bool}]{include\+Children = {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{ordinals_8h_a65e9886d74aaee76545e83dd09011727}{false}}} }\end{DoxyParamCaption}) const}

Returns true if the mouse button is currently held down in this component.

Note that this is a test to see whether the mouse is being pressed in this component, so it\textquotesingle{}ll return false if called on component A when the mouse is actually being dragged in component B.

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily static bool \mbox{\hyperlink{group__juce__core-system_gaf0b3f78ca801d88a7912f4c6bbf50e58}{JUCE\+\_\+\+CALLTYPE}} Component\+::is\+Mouse\+Button\+Down\+Anywhere (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [static]}, {\ttfamily [noexcept]}}

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_a0c7c1ca9e294d4f0ad919e3e7e68dda7}{is\+Mouse\+Button\+Down}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_modifier_keys}{Modifier\+Keys}} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{class_component_adf24c1e586677b3b2acddb71b4ca1ed9}\label{class_component_adf24c1e586677b3b2acddb71b4ca1ed9}} 
\index{Component@{Component}!isMouseOver@{isMouseOver}}
\index{isMouseOver@{isMouseOver}!Component@{Component}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{isMouseOver()}{isMouseOver()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily bool Component\+::is\+Mouse\+Over (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{bool}]{include\+Children = {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{ordinals_8h_a65e9886d74aaee76545e83dd09011727}{false}}} }\end{DoxyParamCaption}) const}

Returns true if the mouse is currently over this component.

If the mouse isn\textquotesingle{}t over the component, this will return false, even if the mouse is currently being dragged -\/ so you can use this in your mouse\+Drag method to find out whether it\textquotesingle{}s really over the component or not.

Note that when the mouse button is being held down, then the only component for which this method will return true is the one that was originally clicked on.

Also note that on a touch-\/screen device, this will only return true when a finger is actually down -\/ as soon as all touch is released, is\+Mouse\+Over will always return false.

If include\+Children is true, then this will also return true if the mouse is over any of the component\textquotesingle{}s children (recursively) as well as the component itself.

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_a0c7c1ca9e294d4f0ad919e3e7e68dda7}{is\+Mouse\+Button\+Down}}. \mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_a67566f891a0b688bfb6ee7b9cdc0b1c9}{is\+Mouse\+Over\+Or\+Dragging}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_aff01e4d339bda474a66984b709044b63}{mouse\+Drag}} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{class_component_a67566f891a0b688bfb6ee7b9cdc0b1c9}\label{class_component_a67566f891a0b688bfb6ee7b9cdc0b1c9}}

\index{isPaintingUnclipped@{isPaintingUnclipped}!Component@{Component}}

\mbox{\Hypertarget{class_component_ab063a5c631854864da09106abec78a86}\label{class_component_ab063a5c631854864da09106abec78a86}} 
\index{Component@{Component}!keyPressed@{keyPressed}}
\index{keyPressed@{keyPressed}!Component@{Component}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{keyPressed()}{keyPressed()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily virtual bool Component\+::key\+Pressed (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{zconf_8in_8h_a2c212835823e3c54a8ab6d95c652660e}{const}} \mbox{\hyperlink{class_key_press}{Key\+Press}} \&}]{key }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [virtual]}}

Called when a key is pressed.

When a key is pressed, the component that has the keyboard focus will have this method called. Remember that a component will only be given the focus if its \mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_a6a1f21a76b971d54870cb5c32c041055}{set\+Wants\+Keyboard\+Focus()}} method has been used to enable this.

If your implementation returns true, the event will be consumed and not passed on to any other listeners. If it returns false, the key will be passed to any Key\+Listeners that have been registered with this component. As soon as one of these returns true, the process will stop, but if they all return false, the event will be passed upwards to this component\textquotesingle{}s parent, and so on.

The default implementation of this method does nothing and returns false.

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_aeff4d2fdbae4d5974e43b62ab3c304f9}{key\+State\+Changed}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_aa056639955cf136ee527e1a7425887b8}{get\+Currently\+Focused\+Component}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_a4ec1b609c39c54434f746cefffa6ce3f}{add\+Key\+Listener}} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}

\index{Component@{Component}!keyStateChanged@{keyStateChanged}}
\index{keyStateChanged@{keyStateChanged}!Component@{Component}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{keyStateChanged()}{keyStateChanged()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily virtual bool Component\+::key\+State\+Changed (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{bool}]{is\+Key\+Down }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [virtual]}}

Called when a key is pressed or released.

Whenever a key on the keyboard is pressed or released (including modifier keys like shift and ctrl), this method will be called on the component that currently has the keyboard focus. Remember that a component will only be given the focus if its \mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_a6a1f21a76b971d54870cb5c32c041055}{set\+Wants\+Keyboard\+Focus()}} method has been used to enable this.

If your implementation returns true, the event will be consumed and not passed on to any other listeners. If it returns false, then any Key\+Listeners that have been registered with this component will have their key\+State\+Changed methods called. As soon as one of these returns true, the process will stop, but if they all return false, the event will be passed upwards to this component\textquotesingle{}s parent, and so on.

The default implementation of this method does nothing and returns false.

To find out which keys are up or down at any time, see the \mbox{\hyperlink{class_key_press_a22dc8e2e91023e57ef9e102aef0c6961}{Key\+Press\+::is\+Key\+Currently\+Down()}} method.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em is\+Key\+Down} & true if a key has been pressed; false if it has been released\\

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{lookAndFeelChanged()}{lookAndFeelChanged()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily virtual \mbox{\hyperlink{png_8h_aa8c59027f9ab2769342f248709d68d17}{void}} Component\+::look\+And\+Feel\+Changed (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [virtual]}}

Called to let the component react to a change in the look-\/and-\/feel setting.

When the look-\/and-\/feel is changed for a component, this will be called in all its child components, recursively.

It can also be triggered manually by the \mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_ac314d2449213d7942eca083addfcd097}{send\+Look\+And\+Feel\+Change()}} method, in case an application uses a \mbox{\hyperlink{class_look_and_feel}{Look\+And\+Feel}} class that might have changed internally.

{\footnotesize\ttfamily virtual \mbox{\hyperlink{png_8h_aa8c59027f9ab2769342f248709d68d17}{void}} Component\+::minimisation\+State\+Changed (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{bool}]{is\+Now\+Minimised }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [virtual]}}

Called for a desktop component which has just been minimised or un-\/minimised. This will only be called for components on the desktop. \begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_a6a137109881ef1e268ee5ec51a633269}{get\+Peer}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_peer_aa9732a41b884d1e8021c69908ed72fdb}{Component\+Peer\+::set\+Minimised}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_peer_a89063a1ab796e670d56ff660c3de60ed}{Component\+Peer\+::is\+Minimised}} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{class_component_a4145c1c28dd2ae42b19c9c3e0a6aba7b}\label{class_component_a4145c1c28dd2ae42b19c9c3e0a6aba7b}} 
\index{Component@{Component}!modifierKeysChanged@{modifierKeysChanged}}
\index{modifierKeysChanged@{modifierKeysChanged}!Component@{Component}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{modifierKeysChanged()}{modifierKeysChanged()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily virtual \mbox{\hyperlink{png_8h_aa8c59027f9ab2769342f248709d68d17}{void}} Component\+::modifier\+Keys\+Changed (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{zconf_8in_8h_a2c212835823e3c54a8ab6d95c652660e}{const}} \mbox{\hyperlink{class_modifier_keys}{Modifier\+Keys}} \&}]{modifiers }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [virtual]}}

Called when a modifier key is pressed or released.

Whenever the shift, control, alt or command keys are pressed or released, this method will be called.

The component that is currently under the main mouse pointer will be tried first and, if there is no component currently under the pointer, the component that currently has the keyboard focus will have this method called. Remember that a component will only be given the focus if its \mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_a6a1f21a76b971d54870cb5c32c041055}{set\+Wants\+Keyboard\+Focus()}} method has been used to enable this.

The default implementation of this method actually calls its parent\textquotesingle{}s modifier\+Keys\+Changed method, so that focused components which aren\textquotesingle{}t interested in this will give their parents a chance to act on the event instead.

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_aeff4d2fdbae4d5974e43b62ab3c304f9}{key\+State\+Changed}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_modifier_keys}{Modifier\+Keys}} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}


Reimplemented in \mbox{\hyperlink{class_slider_a50bfc1f4bc764cd7db7d25abed9e0198}{Slider}}.

\mbox{\Hypertarget{class_component_a6f85fd58365bc184b4cfc0fe09e61696}\label{class_component_a6f85fd58365bc184b4cfc0fe09e61696}} 
\index{Component@{Component}!mouseDoubleClick@{mouseDoubleClick}}
\index{mouseDoubleClick@{mouseDoubleClick}!Component@{Component}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{mouseDoubleClick()}{mouseDoubleClick()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{png_8h_aa8c59027f9ab2769342f248709d68d17}{void}} Component\+::mouse\+Double\+Click (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{zconf_8in_8h_a2c212835823e3c54a8ab6d95c652660e}{const}} \mbox{\hyperlink{class_mouse_event}{Mouse\+Event}} \&}]{event }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [override]}, {\ttfamily [virtual]}}

Called when a mouse button has been double-\/clicked on a component.

The \mbox{\hyperlink{class_mouse_event}{Mouse\+Event}} object passed in contains lots of methods for finding out which button was pressed, as well as which modifier keys (e.\+g. shift, ctrl) were held down at the time.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em event} & details about the position and status of the mouse event, including the source component in which it occurred \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
