\index{Component@{Component}!mouseDown@{mouseDown}}
\index{mouseDown@{mouseDown}!Component@{Component}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{mouseDown()}{mouseDown()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{png_8h_aa8c59027f9ab2769342f248709d68d17}{void}} Component\+::mouse\+Down (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{zconf_8in_8h_a2c212835823e3c54a8ab6d95c652660e}{const}} \mbox{\hyperlink{class_mouse_event}{Mouse\+Event}} \&}]{event }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [override]}, {\ttfamily [virtual]}}

Called when a mouse button is pressed.

The \mbox{\hyperlink{class_mouse_event}{Mouse\+Event}} object passed in contains lots of methods for finding out which button was pressed, as well as which modifier keys (e.\+g. shift, ctrl) were held down at the time.

Once a button is held down, the mouse\+Drag method will be called when the mouse moves, until the button is released.

{\em event} & details about the position and status of the mouse event, including the source component in which it occurred \\

\end{DoxyParams}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{mouseDrag()}{mouseDrag()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{png_8h_aa8c59027f9ab2769342f248709d68d17}{void}} Component\+::mouse\+Drag (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{zconf_8in_8h_a2c212835823e3c54a8ab6d95c652660e}{const}} \mbox{\hyperlink{class_mouse_event}{Mouse\+Event}} \&}]{event }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [override]}, {\ttfamily [virtual]}}

Called when the mouse is moved while a button is held down.

When a mouse button is pressed inside a component, that component receives mouse\+Drag callbacks each time the mouse moves, even if the mouse strays outside the component\textquotesingle{}s bounds.

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{mouseEnter()}{mouseEnter()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{png_8h_aa8c59027f9ab2769342f248709d68d17}{void}} Component\+::mouse\+Enter (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{zconf_8in_8h_a2c212835823e3c54a8ab6d95c652660e}{const}} \mbox{\hyperlink{class_mouse_event}{Mouse\+Event}} \&}]{event }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [override]}, {\ttfamily [virtual]}}

Called when the mouse first enters a component.

If the mouse button isn\textquotesingle{}t pressed and the mouse moves into a component, this will be called to let the component react to this.

When the mouse button is pressed and held down while being moved in or out of a component, no mouse\+Enter or mouse\+Exit callbacks are made -\/ only mouse\+Drag messages are sent to the component that the mouse was originally clicked on, until the button is released.

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{mouseExit()}{mouseExit()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{png_8h_aa8c59027f9ab2769342f248709d68d17}{void}} Component\+::mouse\+Exit (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{zconf_8in_8h_a2c212835823e3c54a8ab6d95c652660e}{const}} \mbox{\hyperlink{class_mouse_event}{Mouse\+Event}} \&}]{event }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [override]}, {\ttfamily [virtual]}}

Called when the mouse moves out of a component.

This will be called when the mouse moves off the edge of this component.

If the mouse button was pressed, and it was then dragged off the edge of the component and released, then this callback will happen when the button is released, after the mouse\+Up callback.

Called when a pinch-\/to-\/zoom mouse-\/gesture is used.

If not overridden, a component will forward this message to its parent, so that parent components can collect gesture messages that are unused by child components.

Called when the mouse moves inside a component.

If the mouse button isn\textquotesingle{}t pressed and the mouse moves over a component, this will be called to let the component react to this.

A component will always get a mouse\+Enter callback before a mouse\+Move.

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{mouseUp()}{mouseUp()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{png_8h_aa8c59027f9ab2769342f248709d68d17}{void}} Component\+::mouse\+Up (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{zconf_8in_8h_a2c212835823e3c54a8ab6d95c652660e}{const}} \mbox{\hyperlink{class_mouse_event}{Mouse\+Event}} \&}]{event }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [override]}, {\ttfamily [virtual]}}

Called when a mouse button is released.

A mouse\+Up callback is sent to the component in which a button was pressed even if the mouse is actually over a different component when the button is released.

The \mbox{\hyperlink{class_mouse_event}{Mouse\+Event}} object passed in contains lots of methods for finding out which buttons were down just before they were released.

\index{Component@{Component}!mouseWheelMove@{mouseWheelMove}}
\index{mouseWheelMove@{mouseWheelMove}!Component@{Component}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{mouseWheelMove()}{mouseWheelMove()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{png_8h_aa8c59027f9ab2769342f248709d68d17}{void}} Component\+::mouse\+Wheel\+Move (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{zconf_8in_8h_a2c212835823e3c54a8ab6d95c652660e}{const}} \mbox{\hyperlink{class_mouse_event}{Mouse\+Event}} \&}]{event,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{zconf_8in_8h_a2c212835823e3c54a8ab6d95c652660e}{const}} \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_mouse_wheel_details}{Mouse\+Wheel\+Details}} \&}]{wheel }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [override]}, {\ttfamily [virtual]}}

Called when the mouse-\/wheel is moved.

This callback is sent to the component that the mouse is over when the wheel is moved.

If not overridden, a component will forward this message to its parent, so that parent components can collect mouse-\/wheel messages that happen to child components which aren\textquotesingle{}t interested in them. (Bear in mind that if you attach a component as a mouse-\/listener to other components, then those wheel moves will also end up calling this method and being passed up to the parents, which may not be what you intended to happen).


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em event} & details about the mouse event \\
\hline
{\em wheel} & details about the mouse wheel movement \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}


Reimplemented from \mbox{\hyperlink{class_mouse_listener_aa3f014806b0820c2b5312553e678e993}{Mouse\+Listener}}.



Reimplemented in \mbox{\hyperlink{class_scroll_bar_a308b14576da7818ec9b1032745b33dc3}{Scroll\+Bar}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_viewport_a80424caacc5b478b1904f3cfcda51cc9}{Viewport}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_combo_box_a48d026065fbdd6822c1d2c07a72aa41b}{Combo\+Box}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_list_box_a2e80ef131eb8e538d1047c4545a63d52}{List\+Box}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_slider_a9b7ee511b24ee74065f92820423f0c46}{Slider}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_text_editor_ac5d9cb318b86e1661d39d65e4cc91aef}{Text\+Editor}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_code_editor_component_a977b36773552d5304aa13cd3d77c1378}{Code\+Editor\+Component}}, and \mbox{\hyperlink{structjuce_1_1_popup_menu_1_1_helper_classes_1_1_menu_window_a65fb2c91c3905658b122dc050af523e1}{juce\+::\+Popup\+Menu\+::\+Helper\+Classes\+::\+Menu\+Window}}.

\mbox{\Hypertarget{class_component_a1b94f2816dc8bc20473620e0db0e8246}\label{class_component_a1b94f2816dc8bc20473620e0db0e8246}} 
\index{Component@{Component}!moved@{moved}}
\index{moved@{moved}!Component@{Component}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{moved()}{moved()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily virtual \mbox{\hyperlink{png_8h_aa8c59027f9ab2769342f248709d68d17}{void}} Component\+::moved (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [virtual]}}

Called when this component\textquotesingle{}s position has been changed.

This is called when the position relative to its parent changes, not when its absolute position on the screen changes (so it won\textquotesingle{}t be called for all child components when a parent component is moved).

The method is called synchronously as a result of the set\+Bounds, set\+Top\+Left\+Position or any of the other repositioning methods, and like \mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_ad896183a68d71daf5816982d1fefd960}{resized()}}, it will be called each time those methods are called.

If the component is a top-\/level window on the desktop, its position could also be changed by operating-\/system factors beyond the application\textquotesingle{}s control.

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_ad896183a68d71daf5816982d1fefd960}{resized}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_a64cbeee83a441e20ed5e7acb600ae107}{set\+Bounds}} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}


Reimplemented in \mbox{\hyperlink{class_side_panel_a02e8ea9c1acae6cbd062916ee89c4431}{Side\+Panel}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_call_out_box_adbe7b39dc2d141143b8168aae6559bfe}{Call\+Out\+Box}}, and \mbox{\hyperlink{class_resizable_window_acfb2ced15e476e78f9a71b0214414798}{Resizable\+Window}}.

\mbox{\Hypertarget{class_component_a2be625dadff73d1ec003cb06749ba6d6}\label{class_component_a2be625dadff73d1ec003cb06749ba6d6}} 
\index{Component@{Component}!moveKeyboardFocusToSibling@{moveKeyboardFocusToSibling}}
\index{moveKeyboardFocusToSibling@{moveKeyboardFocusToSibling}!Component@{Component}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{moveKeyboardFocusToSibling()}{moveKeyboardFocusToSibling()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{png_8h_aa8c59027f9ab2769342f248709d68d17}{void}} Component\+::move\+Keyboard\+Focus\+To\+Sibling (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{bool}]{move\+To\+Next }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Tries to move the keyboard focus to one of this component\textquotesingle{}s siblings.

This will try to move focus to either the next or previous component, as determined by the get\+Next\+Component() and get\+Previous\+Component() implementations of the \mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_traverser}{Component\+Traverser}} returned by \mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_a8dc872ef83fedecd89cf814d28236cd0}{create\+Keyboard\+Focus\+Traverser()}}.

This is the method that is used when shifting focus by pressing the tab key.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em move\+To\+Next} & if true, the focus will move forwards; if false, it will move backwards \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_a91886a0e276d27719fa8866a95306571}{grab\+Keyboard\+Focus}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_a0492ed11cb7fb9102b8284bccb0d9d78}{give\+Away\+Keyboard\+Focus}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_a5c6ce0b41244e147db85274cbac0e84d}{set\+Focus\+Container\+Type}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_a6a1f21a76b971d54870cb5c32c041055}{set\+Wants\+Keyboard\+Focus}} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{class_component_a7cf1862f4af5909ea72827898114a182}\label{class_component_a7cf1862f4af5909ea72827898114a182}} 
\index{Component@{Component}!paint@{paint}}
\index{paint@{paint}!Component@{Component}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{paint()}{paint()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily virtual \mbox{\hyperlink{png_8h_aa8c59027f9ab2769342f248709d68d17}{void}} Component\+::paint (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{class_graphics}{Graphics}} \&}]{g }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [virtual]}}

Components can override this method to draw their content.

The \mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_a7cf1862f4af5909ea72827898114a182}{paint()}} method gets called when a region of a component needs redrawing, either because the component\textquotesingle{}s \mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_af3ab3eabec93dd60faf983370f3a1206}{repaint()}} method has been called, or because something has happened on the screen that means a section of a window needs to be redrawn.

Any child components will draw themselves over whatever this method draws. If you need to paint over the top of your child components, you can also implement the \mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_aa15dc77c06b5a0a4192090b4a323f79c}{paint\+Over\+Children()}} method to do this.

If you want to cause a component to redraw itself, this is done asynchronously -\/ calling the \mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_af3ab3eabec93dd60faf983370f3a1206}{repaint()}} method marks a region of the component as \char`\"{}dirty\char`\"{}, and the \mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_a7cf1862f4af5909ea72827898114a182}{paint()}} method will automatically be called sometime later, by the message thread, to paint any bits that need refreshing. In JUCE (and almost all modern UI frameworks), you never redraw something synchronously.

You should never need to call this method directly -\/ to take a snapshot of the component you could use \mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_a275e46e5a8147f89c142c91ba5c793a5}{create\+Component\+Snapshot()}} or \mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_a2c960bd5ec5ac76d18e82b6883096714}{paint\+Entire\+Component()}}.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em g} & the graphics context that must be used to do the drawing operations. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_af3ab3eabec93dd60faf983370f3a1206}{repaint}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_aa15dc77c06b5a0a4192090b4a323f79c}{paint\+Over\+Children}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_graphics}{Graphics}} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}

\index{Component@{Component}!paintEntireComponent@{paintEntireComponent}}
\index{paintEntireComponent@{paintEntireComponent}!Component@{Component}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{paintEntireComponent()}{paintEntireComponent()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{png_8h_aa8c59027f9ab2769342f248709d68d17}{void}} Component\+::paint\+Entire\+Component (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{class_graphics}{Graphics}} \&}]{context,  }\item[{bool}]{ignore\+Alpha\+Level }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Draws this component and all its subcomponents onto the specified graphics context.

You should very rarely have to use this method, it\textquotesingle{}s simply there in case you need to draw a component with a custom graphics context for some reason, e.\+g. for creating a snapshot of the component.

It calls \mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_a7cf1862f4af5909ea72827898114a182}{paint()}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_aa15dc77c06b5a0a4192090b4a323f79c}{paint\+Over\+Children()}} and recursively calls \mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_a2c960bd5ec5ac76d18e82b6883096714}{paint\+Entire\+Component()}} on its children in order to render the entire tree.

The graphics context may be left in an undefined state after this method returns, so you may need to reset it if you\textquotesingle{}re going to use it again.

If ignore\+Alpha\+Level is false, then the component will be drawn with the opacity level specified by \mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_a1fa7fae9983fed145b733d809dc7b2e5}{get\+Alpha()}}; if ignore\+Alpha\+Level is true, then this will be ignored and an alpha of 1.\+0 will be used. \mbox{\Hypertarget{class_component_aa15dc77c06b5a0a4192090b4a323f79c}\label{class_component_aa15dc77c06b5a0a4192090b4a323f79c}} 
\index{Component@{Component}!paintOverChildren@{paintOverChildren}}
\index{paintOverChildren@{paintOverChildren}!Component@{Component}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{paintOverChildren()}{paintOverChildren()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily virtual \mbox{\hyperlink{png_8h_aa8c59027f9ab2769342f248709d68d17}{void}} Component\+::paint\+Over\+Children (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{class_graphics}{Graphics}} \&}]{g }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [virtual]}}

Components can override this method to draw over the top of their children.

For most drawing operations, it\textquotesingle{}s better to use the normal \mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_a7cf1862f4af5909ea72827898114a182}{paint()}} method, but if you need to overlay something on top of the children, this can be used.

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_a7cf1862f4af5909ea72827898114a182}{paint}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_graphics}{Graphics}} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}

\index{Component@{Component}!parentHierarchyChanged@{parentHierarchyChanged}}
\index{parentHierarchyChanged@{parentHierarchyChanged}!Component@{Component}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{parentHierarchyChanged()}{parentHierarchyChanged()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily virtual \mbox{\hyperlink{png_8h_aa8c59027f9ab2769342f248709d68d17}{void}} Component\+::parent\+Hierarchy\+Changed (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [virtual]}}

Called to indicate that the component\textquotesingle{}s parents have changed.

When a component is added or removed from its parent, this method will be called on all of its children (recursively -\/ so all children of its children will also be called as well).

Subclasses can override this if they need to react to this in some way.

\index{Component@{Component}!postCommandMessage@{postCommandMessage}}
\index{postCommandMessage@{postCommandMessage}!Component@{Component}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{postCommandMessage()}{postCommandMessage()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{png_8h_aa8c59027f9ab2769342f248709d68d17}{void}} Component\+::post\+Command\+Message (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group__juce__audio__plugin__client-_unity_ga966b05a42d98c7296097e073c627dcd0}{int}}}]{command\+Id }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Dispatches a numbered message to this component.

This is a quick and cheap way of allowing simple asynchronous messages to be sent to components. It\textquotesingle{}s also safe, because if the component that you send the message to is a null or dangling pointer, this won\textquotesingle{}t cause an error.

The command ID is later delivered to the component\textquotesingle{}s \mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_a9ba6fa31d1397c7e90050b2cd4f2089b}{handle\+Command\+Message()}} method by the application\textquotesingle{}s message queue.

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_a9ba6fa31d1397c7e90050b2cd4f2089b}{handle\+Command\+Message}} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}

To do that, use \mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_abc8f8338a400c20d5e941ea3a1f67f7b}{delete\+All\+Children()}} instead. \mbox{\Hypertarget{class_component_a221324c67c9fb048895b8730dbf1b642}\label{class_component_a221324c67c9fb048895b8730dbf1b642}} 
\index{Component@{Component}!removeChildComponent@{removeChildComponent}}
\index{removeChildComponent@{removeChildComponent}!Component@{Component}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{removeChildComponent()}{removeChildComponent()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{png_8h_aa8c59027f9ab2769342f248709d68d17}{void}} Component\+::remove\+Child\+Component (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{class_component}{Component}} $\ast$}]{child\+To\+Remove }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Removes one of this component\textquotesingle{}s child-\/components.

If the child passed-\/in isn\textquotesingle{}t actually a child of this component (either because it\textquotesingle{}s invalid or is the child of a different parent), then no action is taken.

Note that removing a child will not delete it! But it\textquotesingle{}s ok to delete a component without first removing it -\/ doing so will automatically remove it and send out the appropriate notifications before the deletion completes.

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}

Removes one of this component\textquotesingle{}s child-\/components by index.

This will return a pointer to the component that was removed, or null if the index was out-\/of-\/range.

Note that removing a child will not delete it! But it\textquotesingle{}s ok to delete a component without first removing it -\/ doing so will automatically remove it and send out the appropriate notifications before the deletion completes.

If the component is currently showing on the desktop, this will hide it.

You can also use \mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_ac8483af6fe4dc3254e7176df0d8e9f7a}{set\+Visible()}} to hide a desktop window temporarily, but \mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_a3eb22f7e39f71fdad3e84a8700807a82}{remove\+From\+Desktop()}} will free any system resources that are being used up.

\index{Component@{Component}!repaint@{repaint}}
\index{repaint@{repaint}!Component@{Component}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{repaint()}{repaint()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/3]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{png_8h_aa8c59027f9ab2769342f248709d68d17}{void}} Component\+::repaint (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Marks the whole component as needing to be redrawn.

Calling this will not do any repainting immediately, but will mark the component as \textquotesingle{}dirty\textquotesingle{}. At some point in the near future the operating system will send a paint message, which will redraw all the dirty regions of all components. There\textquotesingle{}s no guarantee about how soon after calling \mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_af3ab3eabec93dd60faf983370f3a1206}{repaint()}} the redraw will actually happen, and other queued events may be delivered before a redraw is done.

If the \mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_af19bbc2186e3297ddd55c328e46c014b}{set\+Buffered\+To\+Image()}} method has been used to cause this component to use a buffer, the \mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_af3ab3eabec93dd60faf983370f3a1206}{repaint()}} call will invalidate the cached buffer. If \mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_a9a19c5cf59573243d77a94bb3abea722}{set\+Cached\+Component\+Image()}} has been used to provide a custom image cache, that cache will be invalidated appropriately.

To redraw just a subsection of the component rather than the whole thing, use the repaint (int, int, int, int) method.

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_a7cf1862f4af5909ea72827898114a182}{paint}} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{class_component_af2a079621367cdf3755d708b4dbbc820}\label{class_component_af2a079621367cdf3755d708b4dbbc820}} 
\index{Component@{Component}!repaint@{repaint}}
\index{repaint@{repaint}!Component@{Component}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{repaint()}{repaint()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [2/3]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{png_8h_aa8c59027f9ab2769342f248709d68d17}{void}} Component\+::repaint (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group__juce__audio__plugin__client-_unity_ga966b05a42d98c7296097e073c627dcd0}{int}}}]{x,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group__juce__audio__plugin__client-_unity_ga966b05a42d98c7296097e073c627dcd0}{int}}}]{y,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group__juce__audio__plugin__client-_unity_ga966b05a42d98c7296097e073c627dcd0}{int}}}]{width,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group__juce__audio__plugin__client-_unity_ga966b05a42d98c7296097e073c627dcd0}{int}}}]{height }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Marks a subsection of this component as needing to be redrawn.

Calling this will not do any repainting immediately, but will mark the given region of the component as \textquotesingle{}dirty\textquotesingle{}. At some point in the near future the operating system will send a paint message, which will redraw all the dirty regions of all components. There\textquotesingle{}s no guarantee about how soon after calling \mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_af3ab3eabec93dd60faf983370f3a1206}{repaint()}} the redraw will actually happen, and other queued events may be delivered before a redraw is done.

The region that is passed in will be clipped to keep it within the bounds of this component.

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_af3ab3eabec93dd60faf983370f3a1206}{repaint()}} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}

\index{Component@{Component}!repaint@{repaint}}
\index{repaint@{repaint}!Component@{Component}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{repaint()}{repaint()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [3/3]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{png_8h_aa8c59027f9ab2769342f248709d68d17}{void}} Component\+::repaint (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{class_rectangle}{Rectangle}}$<$ \mbox{\hyperlink{group__juce__audio__plugin__client-_unity_ga966b05a42d98c7296097e073c627dcd0}{int}} $>$}]{area }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Marks a subsection of this component as needing to be redrawn.

Calling this will not do any repainting immediately, but will mark the given region of the component as \textquotesingle{}dirty\textquotesingle{}. At some point in the near future the operating system will send a paint message, which will redraw all the dirty regions of all components. There\textquotesingle{}s no guarantee about how soon after calling \mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_af3ab3eabec93dd60faf983370f3a1206}{repaint()}} the redraw will actually happen, and other queued events may be delivered before a redraw is done.

The region that is passed in will be clipped to keep it within the bounds of this component.

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_af3ab3eabec93dd60faf983370f3a1206}{repaint()}} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{class_component_ad896183a68d71daf5816982d1fefd960}\label{class_component_ad896183a68d71daf5816982d1fefd960}} 
\index{Component@{Component}!resized@{resized}}
\index{resized@{resized}!Component@{Component}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{resized()}{resized()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily virtual \mbox{\hyperlink{png_8h_aa8c59027f9ab2769342f248709d68d17}{void}} Component\+::resized (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [virtual]}}

Called when this component\textquotesingle{}s size has been changed.

A component can implement this method to do things such as laying out its child components when its width or height changes.

The method is called synchronously as a result of the set\+Bounds or set\+Size methods, so repeatedly changing a components size will repeatedly call its resized method (unlike things like repainting, where multiple calls to repaint are coalesced together).

If the component is a top-\/level window on the desktop, its size could also be changed by operating-\/system factors beyond the application\textquotesingle{}s control.

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_a1b94f2816dc8bc20473620e0db0e8246}{moved}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_af7e0443344448fcbbefc2b3dd985e43f}{set\+Size}} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}

\index{Component@{Component}!sendLookAndFeelChange@{sendLookAndFeelChange}}
\index{sendLookAndFeelChange@{sendLookAndFeelChange}!Component@{Component}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{sendLookAndFeelChange()}{sendLookAndFeelChange()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{png_8h_aa8c59027f9ab2769342f248709d68d17}{void}} Component\+::send\+Look\+And\+Feel\+Change (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Calls the \mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_a74af5830b815f6f985768a5673d01cf2}{look\+And\+Feel\+Changed()}} method in this component and all its children.

This will recurse through the children and their children, calling \mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_a74af5830b815f6f985768a5673d01cf2}{look\+And\+Feel\+Changed()}} on them all.

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_a74af5830b815f6f985768a5673d01cf2}{look\+And\+Feel\+Changed}} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{class_component_a8d86a21c61518203b42766303cdb019e}\label{class_component_a8d86a21c61518203b42766303cdb019e}} 
\index{Component@{Component}!setAccessible@{setAccessible}}
\index{setAccessible@{setAccessible}!Component@{Component}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{setAccessible()}{setAccessible()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{png_8h_aa8c59027f9ab2769342f248709d68d17}{void}} Component\+::set\+Accessible (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{bool}]{should\+Be\+Accessible }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Sets whether this component and its children are visible to accessibility clients.

If this flag is set to false then the \mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_a31bd71686e3d54ff55fbf4514768d735}{get\+Accessibility\+Handler()}} method will return nullptr and this component and its children will not be visible to any accessibility clients.

By default this is set to true.

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_ab06d8f631df630c8a194e742010f1c66}{is\+Accessible}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_a31bd71686e3d54ff55fbf4514768d735}{get\+Accessibility\+Handler}} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}

\index{Component@{Component}!setAlpha@{setAlpha}}
\index{setAlpha@{setAlpha}!Component@{Component}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{setAlpha()}{setAlpha()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{png_8h_aa8c59027f9ab2769342f248709d68d17}{void}} Component\+::set\+Alpha (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{float}]{new\+Alpha }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Changes the transparency of this component. When painted, the entire component and all its children will be rendered with this as the overall opacity level, where 0 is completely invisible, and 1.\+0 is fully opaque (i.\+e. normal).

\index{Component@{Component}!setAlwaysOnTop@{setAlwaysOnTop}}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{setAlwaysOnTop()}{setAlwaysOnTop()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{png_8h_aa8c59027f9ab2769342f248709d68d17}{void}} Component\+::set\+Always\+On\+Top (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{bool}]{should\+Stay\+On\+Top }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Sets whether the component should always be kept at the front of its siblings. \begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}

\mbox{\Hypertarget{class_component_a64cbeee83a441e20ed5e7acb600ae107}\label{class_component_a64cbeee83a441e20ed5e7acb600ae107}} 
\index{Component@{Component}!setBounds@{setBounds}}
\index{setBounds@{setBounds}!Component@{Component}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{setBounds()}{setBounds()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{png_8h_aa8c59027f9ab2769342f248709d68d17}{void}} Component\+::set\+Bounds (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group__juce__audio__plugin__client-_unity_ga966b05a42d98c7296097e073c627dcd0}{int}}}]{x,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group__juce__audio__plugin__client-_unity_ga966b05a42d98c7296097e073c627dcd0}{int}}}]{y,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group__juce__audio__plugin__client-_unity_ga966b05a42d98c7296097e073c627dcd0}{int}}}]{width,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group__juce__audio__plugin__client-_unity_ga966b05a42d98c7296097e073c627dcd0}{int}}}]{height }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Changes the component\textquotesingle{}s position and size.

The coordinates are relative to the top-\/left of the component\textquotesingle{}s parent, or relative to the origin of the screen if the component is on the desktop.

If this method changes the component\textquotesingle{}s top-\/left position, it will make a synchronous call to \mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_a1b94f2816dc8bc20473620e0db0e8246}{moved()}}. If it changes the size, it will also make a call to \mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_ad896183a68d71daf5816982d1fefd960}{resized()}}.

Note that if you\textquotesingle{}ve used \mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_a42d13229962acb1cdf4328c4a490ffef}{set\+Transform()}} to apply a transform, then the component\textquotesingle{}s bounds will no longer be a direct reflection of the position at which it appears within its parent, as the transform will be applied to whatever bounds you set for it.

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_a46f3b243e2ff2d000285c8642be7ea0a}{set\+Top\+Left\+Position}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_af7e0443344448fcbbefc2b3dd985e43f}{set\+Size}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_listener_a95adb1bc55096aefa74f9033be32aa47}{Component\+Listener\+::component\+Moved\+Or\+Resized}} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{class_component_a1bd97a58b5ab72b3e803c6b90a41ea4f}\label{class_component_a1bd97a58b5ab72b3e803c6b90a41ea4f}} 
\index{Component@{Component}!setBounds@{setBounds}}
\index{setBounds@{setBounds}!Component@{Component}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{setBounds()}{setBounds()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [2/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{png_8h_aa8c59027f9ab2769342f248709d68d17}{void}} Component\+::set\+Bounds (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{class_rectangle}{Rectangle}}$<$ \mbox{\hyperlink{group__juce__audio__plugin__client-_unity_ga966b05a42d98c7296097e073c627dcd0}{int}} $>$}]{new\+Bounds }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Changes the component\textquotesingle{}s position and size.

The coordinates are relative to the top-\/left of the component\textquotesingle{}s parent, or relative to the origin of the screen if the component is on the desktop.

If this method changes the component\textquotesingle{}s top-\/left position, it will make a synchronous call to \mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_a1b94f2816dc8bc20473620e0db0e8246}{moved()}}. If it changes the size, it will also make a call to \mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_ad896183a68d71daf5816982d1fefd960}{resized()}}.

Note that if you\textquotesingle{}ve used \mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_a42d13229962acb1cdf4328c4a490ffef}{set\+Transform()}} to apply a transform, then the component\textquotesingle{}s bounds will no longer be a direct reflection of the position at which it appears within its parent, as the transform will be applied to whatever bounds you set for it.

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_a64cbeee83a441e20ed5e7acb600ae107}{set\+Bounds}} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}

\index{Component@{Component}!setBoundsInset@{setBoundsInset}}
\index{setBoundsInset@{setBoundsInset}!Component@{Component}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{setBoundsInset()}{setBoundsInset()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{png_8h_aa8c59027f9ab2769342f248709d68d17}{void}} Component\+::set\+Bounds\+Inset (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{class_border_size}{Border\+Size}}$<$ \mbox{\hyperlink{group__juce__audio__plugin__client-_unity_ga966b05a42d98c7296097e073c627dcd0}{int}} $>$}]{borders }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Changes the component\textquotesingle{}s position and size based on the amount of space to leave around it.

This will position the component within its parent, leaving the specified number of pixels around each edge.

\end{DoxySeeAlso}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{class_component_a8752a76d1d0b2b27af1da1169ed5c534}\label{class_component_a8752a76d1d0b2b27af1da1169ed5c534}} 
\index{Component@{Component}!setBoundsRelative@{setBoundsRelative}}
\index{setBoundsRelative@{setBoundsRelative}!Component@{Component}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{setBoundsRelative()}{setBoundsRelative()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{png_8h_aa8c59027f9ab2769342f248709d68d17}{void}} Component\+::set\+Bounds\+Relative (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{float}]{proportionalX,  }\item[{float}]{proportionalY,  }\item[{float}]{proportional\+Width,  }\item[{float}]{proportional\+Height }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Changes the component\textquotesingle{}s position and size in terms of fractions of its parent\textquotesingle{}s size.

The values are factors of the parent\textquotesingle{}s size, so for example set\+Bounds\+Relative (0.\+2f, 0.\+2f, 0.\+5f, 0.\+5f) would give it half the width and height of the parent, with its top-\/left position 20\% of the way across and down the parent.

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_a64cbeee83a441e20ed5e7acb600ae107}{set\+Bounds}} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{class_component_a477d1b81c9cef4d47f1499364928d4ab}\label{class_component_a477d1b81c9cef4d47f1499364928d4ab}} 
\index{Component@{Component}!setBoundsRelative@{setBoundsRelative}}
\index{setBoundsRelative@{setBoundsRelative}!Component@{Component}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{setBoundsRelative()}{setBoundsRelative()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [2/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{png_8h_aa8c59027f9ab2769342f248709d68d17}{void}} Component\+::set\+Bounds\+Relative (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{class_rectangle}{Rectangle}}$<$ float $>$}]{proportional\+Area }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Changes the component\textquotesingle{}s position and size in terms of fractions of its parent\textquotesingle{}s size.

The values are factors of the parent\textquotesingle{}s size, so for example set\+Bounds\+Relative (\{ 0.\+2f, 0.\+2f, 0.\+5f, 0.\+5f \}) would give it half the width and height of the parent, with its top-\/left position 20\% of the way across and down the parent.

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}

\end{DoxySeeAlso}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{class_component_a321834a9260001deb8dbd446d59e452f}\label{class_component_a321834a9260001deb8dbd446d59e452f}} 
\index{Component@{Component}!setBoundsToFit@{setBoundsToFit}}
\index{setBoundsToFit@{setBoundsToFit}!Component@{Component}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{setBoundsToFit()}{setBoundsToFit()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{png_8h_aa8c59027f9ab2769342f248709d68d17}{void}} Component\+::set\+Bounds\+To\+Fit (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{class_rectangle}{Rectangle}}$<$ \mbox{\hyperlink{group__juce__audio__plugin__client-_unity_ga966b05a42d98c7296097e073c627dcd0}{int}} $>$}]{target\+Area,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{class_justification}{Justification}}}]{justification,  }\item[{bool}]{only\+Reduce\+In\+Size }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Positions the component within a given rectangle, keeping its proportions unchanged.

If only\+Reduce\+In\+Size is false, the component will be resized to fill as much of the rectangle as possible without changing its aspect ratio (the component\textquotesingle{}s current size is used to determine its aspect ratio, so a zero-\/size component won\textquotesingle{}t work here). If only\+Reduce\+In\+Size is true, it will only be resized if it\textquotesingle{}s too big to fit inside the rectangle.

It will then be positioned within the rectangle according to the justification flags specified.

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_a64cbeee83a441e20ed5e7acb600ae107}{set\+Bounds}} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{class_component_a2e31d54832bfa8b916fef77c4d9eb649}\label{class_component_a2e31d54832bfa8b916fef77c4d9eb649}} 
\index{Component@{Component}!setBroughtToFrontOnMouseClick@{setBroughtToFrontOnMouseClick}}
\index{setBroughtToFrontOnMouseClick@{setBroughtToFrontOnMouseClick}!Component@{Component}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{setBroughtToFrontOnMouseClick()}{setBroughtToFrontOnMouseClick()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{png_8h_aa8c59027f9ab2769342f248709d68d17}{void}} Component\+::set\+Brought\+To\+Front\+On\+Mouse\+Click (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{bool}]{should\+Be\+Brought\+To\+Front }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [noexcept]}}

Indicates whether the component should be brought to the front when clicked.

Setting this flag to true will cause the component to be brought to the front when the mouse is clicked somewhere inside it or its child components.

Note that a top-\/level desktop window might still be brought to the front by the operating system when it\textquotesingle{}s clicked, depending on how the OS works.

By default this is set to false.

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_a5e27530ab343f52b524c1c3f1a1d98eb}{set\+Mouse\+Click\+Grabs\+Keyboard\+Focus}} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{class_component_af19bbc2186e3297ddd55c328e46c014b}\label{class_component_af19bbc2186e3297ddd55c328e46c014b}} 
\index{Component@{Component}!setBufferedToImage@{setBufferedToImage}}
\index{setBufferedToImage@{setBufferedToImage}!Component@{Component}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{setBufferedToImage()}{setBufferedToImage()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{png_8h_aa8c59027f9ab2769342f248709d68d17}{void}} Component\+::set\+Buffered\+To\+Image (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{bool}]{should\+Be\+Buffered }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Makes the component use an internal buffer to optimise its redrawing.

Setting this flag to true will cause the component to allocate an internal buffer into which it paints itself and all its child components, so that when asked to redraw itself, it can use this buffer rather than actually calling the \mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_a7cf1862f4af5909ea72827898114a182}{paint()}} method.

Parts of the buffer are invalidated when \mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_af3ab3eabec93dd60faf983370f3a1206}{repaint()}} is called on this component or its children. The buffer is then repainted at the next \mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_a7cf1862f4af5909ea72827898114a182}{paint()}} callback.

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_af3ab3eabec93dd60faf983370f3a1206}{repaint}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_a7cf1862f4af5909ea72827898114a182}{paint}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_a275e46e5a8147f89c142c91ba5c793a5}{create\+Component\+Snapshot}} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{class_component_a9a19c5cf59573243d77a94bb3abea722}\label{class_component_a9a19c5cf59573243d77a94bb3abea722}}

\index{Component@{Component}!setColour@{setColour}}
\index{setColour@{setColour}!Component@{Component}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{setColour()}{setColour()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{png_8h_aa8c59027f9ab2769342f248709d68d17}{void}} Component\+::set\+Colour (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group__juce__audio__plugin__client-_unity_ga966b05a42d98c7296097e073c627dcd0}{int}}}]{colour\+ID,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{class_colour}{Colour}}}]{new\+Colour }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Registers a colour to be used for a particular purpose.

Changing a colour will cause a synchronous callback to the \mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_adfab11b32c622b327a823c6565f637f4}{colour\+Changed()}} method, which your component can override if it needs to do something when colours are altered.

For more details about colour IDs, see the comments for \mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_a743504b7a85b697404bf9aab17324265}{find\+Colour()}}.

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}

\end{DoxySeeAlso}

\index{Component@{Component}!setComponentEffect@{setComponentEffect}}
\index{setComponentEffect@{setComponentEffect}!Component@{Component}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{setComponentEffect()}{setComponentEffect()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{png_8h_aa8c59027f9ab2769342f248709d68d17}{void}} Component\+::set\+Component\+Effect (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{class_image_effect_filter}{Image\+Effect\+Filter}} $\ast$}]{new\+Effect }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Adds an effect filter to alter the component\textquotesingle{}s appearance.

When a component has an effect filter set, then this is applied to the results of its \mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_a7cf1862f4af5909ea72827898114a182}{paint()}} method. There are a few preset effects, such as a drop-\/shadow or glow, but they can be user-\/defined as well.

The effect that is passed in will not be deleted by the component -\/ the caller must take care of deleting it.

To remove an effect from a component, pass a null pointer in as the parameter.

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\mbox{\hyperlink{class_image_effect_filter}{Image\+Effect\+Filter}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_drop_shadow_effect}{Drop\+Shadow\+Effect}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_glow_effect}{Glow\+Effect}} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}

\index{setEnabled@{setEnabled}!Component@{Component}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{setEnabled()}{setEnabled()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{png_8h_aa8c59027f9ab2769342f248709d68d17}{void}} Component\+::set\+Enabled (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{bool}]{should\+Be\+Enabled }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Enables or disables this component.

Disabling a component will also cause all of its child components to become disabled.

Similarly, enabling a component which is inside a disabled parent component won\textquotesingle{}t make any difference until the parent is re-\/enabled.

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}

\index{Component@{Component}!setExplicitFocusOrder@{setExplicitFocusOrder}}
\index{setExplicitFocusOrder@{setExplicitFocusOrder}!Component@{Component}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{setExplicitFocusOrder()}{setExplicitFocusOrder()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{png_8h_aa8c59027f9ab2769342f248709d68d17}{void}} Component\+::set\+Explicit\+Focus\+Order (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group__juce__audio__plugin__client-_unity_ga966b05a42d98c7296097e073c627dcd0}{int}}}]{new\+Focus\+Order\+Index }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Sets the focus order of this component.

The focus order is used by the default traverser implementation returned by \mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_a138dc2e3c7f4836d7c127409dab8a56d}{create\+Focus\+Traverser()}} as part of its algorithm for deciding the order in which components should be traversed. A value of 0 or less is taken to mean that no explicit order is wanted, and that traversal should use other factors, like the component\textquotesingle{}s position.

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_a1ae06fca382eed7ee555d194d947c350}{get\+Explicit\+Focus\+Order}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_focus_traverser}{Focus\+Traverser}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_a138dc2e3c7f4836d7c127409dab8a56d}{create\+Focus\+Traverser}} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{setHasFocusOutline()}{setHasFocusOutline()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{png_8h_aa8c59027f9ab2769342f248709d68d17}{void}} Component\+::set\+Has\+Focus\+Outline (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{bool}]{has\+Focus\+Outline }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}, {\ttfamily [noexcept]}}

Use this to indicate that the component should have an outline drawn around it when it has keyboard focus.

If this is set to true, then when the component gains keyboard focus the \mbox{\hyperlink{class_look_and_feel_a39f2061a27e007e214a607dbf0e31baf}{Look\+And\+Feel\+::create\+Focus\+Outline\+For\+Component()}} method will be used to draw an outline around it.

\index{Component@{Component}!setInterceptsMouseClicks@{setInterceptsMouseClicks}}
\index{setInterceptsMouseClicks@{setInterceptsMouseClicks}!Component@{Component}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{setInterceptsMouseClicks()}{setInterceptsMouseClicks()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{png_8h_aa8c59027f9ab2769342f248709d68d17}{void}} Component\+::set\+Intercepts\+Mouse\+Clicks (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{bool}]{allow\+Clicks\+On\+This\+Component,  }\item[{bool}]{allow\+Clicks\+On\+Child\+Components }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [noexcept]}}

Changes the default return value for the \mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_a2da9631236e1cbf1b340454209a6c9e0}{hit\+Test()}} method.

Setting this to false is an easy way to make a component pass all its mouse events (not just clicks) through to the components behind it.

When a component is created, the default setting for this is true.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em allow\+Clicks\+On\+This\+Component} & if true, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_a2da9631236e1cbf1b340454209a6c9e0}{hit\+Test()}} will always return true; if false, it will return false (or true for child components if allow\+Clicks\+On\+Child\+Components is true) \\
\hline
{\em allow\+Clicks\+On\+Child\+Components} & if this is true and allow\+Clicks\+On\+This\+Component is false, then child components can be clicked on as normal but clicks on this component pass straight through; if this is false and allow\+Clicks\+On\+This\+Component is false, then neither this component nor any child components can be clicked on \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_a2da9631236e1cbf1b340454209a6c9e0}{hit\+Test}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_a219f9c96e896dfbbe3fb967a57297f14}{get\+Intercepts\+Mouse\+Clicks}} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}

\index{Component@{Component}!setLookAndFeel@{setLookAndFeel}}
\index{setLookAndFeel@{setLookAndFeel}!Component@{Component}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{setLookAndFeel()}{setLookAndFeel()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{png_8h_aa8c59027f9ab2769342f248709d68d17}{void}} Component\+::set\+Look\+And\+Feel (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{class_look_and_feel}{Look\+And\+Feel}} $\ast$}]{new\+Look\+And\+Feel }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Sets the look and feel to use for this component.

This will also change the look and feel for any child components that haven\textquotesingle{}t had their look set explicitly.

The object passed in will not be deleted by the component, so it\textquotesingle{}s the caller\textquotesingle{}s responsibility to manage it. It may be used at any time until this component has been deleted.

Calling this method will also invoke the \mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_ac314d2449213d7942eca083addfcd097}{send\+Look\+And\+Feel\+Change()}} method.

\mbox{\Hypertarget{class_component_a7320d543cba40183c894474ab78798ea}\label{class_component_a7320d543cba40183c894474ab78798ea}} 
\index{Component@{Component}!setOpaque@{setOpaque}}
\index{setOpaque@{setOpaque}!Component@{Component}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{setOpaque()}{setOpaque()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{png_8h_aa8c59027f9ab2769342f248709d68d17}{void}} Component\+::set\+Opaque (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{bool}]{should\+Be\+Opaque }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Indicates whether any parts of the component might be transparent.

Components that always paint all of their contents with solid colour and thus completely cover any components behind them should use this method to tell the repaint system that they are opaque.

This information is used to optimise drawing, because it means that objects underneath opaque windows don\textquotesingle{}t need to be painted.

By default, components are considered transparent, unless this is used to make it otherwise.

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_a6ef077ace37bcd13d033305e8875d4e7}{is\+Opaque}} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{class_component_afd2216ecd5029923097d6baabab400ec}\label{class_component_afd2216ecd5029923097d6baabab400ec}} 
\index{Component@{Component}!setPaintingIsUnclipped@{setPaintingIsUnclipped}}
\index{setPaintingIsUnclipped@{setPaintingIsUnclipped}!Component@{Component}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{setPaintingIsUnclipped()}{setPaintingIsUnclipped()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{png_8h_aa8c59027f9ab2769342f248709d68d17}{void}} Component\+::set\+Painting\+Is\+Unclipped (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{bool}]{should\+Paint\+Without\+Clipping }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [noexcept]}}

This allows you to indicate that this component doesn\textquotesingle{}t require its graphics context to be clipped when it is being painted.

Most people will never need to use this setting, but in situations where you have a very large number of simple components being rendered, and where they are guaranteed never to do any drawing beyond their own boundaries, setting this to true will reduce the overhead involved in clipping the graphics context that gets passed to the component\textquotesingle{}s \mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_a7cf1862f4af5909ea72827898114a182}{paint()}} callback. If you enable this mode, you\textquotesingle{}ll need to make sure your paint method doesn\textquotesingle{}t call anything like \mbox{\hyperlink{class_graphics_a46fc8346e7c7c7cc6c9ff2aad76fa442}{Graphics\+::fill\+All()}}, and doesn\textquotesingle{}t draw beyond the component\textquotesingle{}s bounds, because that\textquotesingle{}ll produce artifacts. Your component also can\textquotesingle{}t have any child components that may be placed beyond its bounds. \mbox{\Hypertarget{class_component_a27359d626e9ab896af71cd57c1ff0915}\label{class_component_a27359d626e9ab896af71cd57c1ff0915}} 
\index{Component@{Component}!setPositioner@{setPositioner}}
\index{setPositioner@{setPositioner}!Component@{Component}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{setPositioner()}{setPositioner()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{png_8h_aa8c59027f9ab2769342f248709d68d17}{void}} Component\+::set\+Positioner (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_1_1_positioner}{Positioner}} $\ast$}]{new\+Positioner }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Sets a new \mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_1_1_positioner}{Positioner}} object for this component. If there\textquotesingle{}s currently another positioner set, it will be deleted. The object that is passed in will be deleted automatically by this component when it\textquotesingle{}s no longer required. Pass a null pointer to clear the current positioner. \begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_a2289646e0bd01afc059a0c848438a076}{get\+Positioner()}} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{class_component_a7845e402a21d2b86d8c4ec48bc7c93b1}\label{class_component_a7845e402a21d2b86d8c4ec48bc7c93b1}} 
\index{Component@{Component}!setRepaintsOnMouseActivity@{setRepaintsOnMouseActivity}}
\index{setRepaintsOnMouseActivity@{setRepaintsOnMouseActivity}!Component@{Component}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{setRepaintsOnMouseActivity()}{setRepaintsOnMouseActivity()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{png_8h_aa8c59027f9ab2769342f248709d68d17}{void}} Component\+::set\+Repaints\+On\+Mouse\+Activity (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{bool}]{should\+Repaint }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [noexcept]}}

Causes automatic repaints when the mouse enters or exits this component.

If turned on, then when the mouse enters/exits, or when the button is pressed/released on the component, it will trigger a repaint.

This is handy for things like buttons that need to draw themselves differently when the mouse moves over them, and it avoids having to override all the different mouse callbacks and call \mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_af3ab3eabec93dd60faf983370f3a1206}{repaint()}}.

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_ae9c5746cf4e82c76d063aa0489e45a81}{mouse\+Enter}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_a3d26d32c19eddbfcfbe60f522a137ba5}{mouse\+Exit}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_a2a908e064b0bfed1ea0a75b0a0fee6dd}{mouse\+Down}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_af32dfbd920a1da48ad0d87bdbcda6f70}{mouse\+Up}} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}

\index{Component@{Component}!setTopLeftPosition@{setTopLeftPosition}}
\index{setTopLeftPosition@{setTopLeftPosition}!Component@{Component}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{setTopLeftPosition()}{setTopLeftPosition()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{png_8h_aa8c59027f9ab2769342f248709d68d17}{void}} Component\+::set\+Top\+Left\+Position (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group__juce__audio__plugin__client-_unity_ga966b05a42d98c7296097e073c627dcd0}{int}}}]{x,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group__juce__audio__plugin__client-_unity_ga966b05a42d98c7296097e073c627dcd0}{int}}}]{y }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Moves the component to a new position.

Changes the component\textquotesingle{}s top-\/left position (without changing its size). The position is relative to the top-\/left of the component\textquotesingle{}s parent.

If the component actually moves, this method will make a synchronous call to \mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_a1b94f2816dc8bc20473620e0db0e8246}{moved()}}.

Note that if you\textquotesingle{}ve used \mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_a42d13229962acb1cdf4328c4a490ffef}{set\+Transform()}} to apply a transform, then the component\textquotesingle{}s bounds will no longer be a direct reflection of the position at which it appears within its parent, as the transform will be applied to whatever bounds you set for it.

\end{DoxySeeAlso}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{class_component_a5c86db4e969d69acc78ea3ee899cedff}\label{class_component_a5c86db4e969d69acc78ea3ee899cedff}} 
\index{Component@{Component}!setTopLeftPosition@{setTopLeftPosition}}
\index{setTopLeftPosition@{setTopLeftPosition}!Component@{Component}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{setTopLeftPosition()}{setTopLeftPosition()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [2/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{png_8h_aa8c59027f9ab2769342f248709d68d17}{void}} Component\+::set\+Top\+Left\+Position (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{class_point}{Point}}$<$ \mbox{\hyperlink{group__juce__audio__plugin__client-_unity_ga966b05a42d98c7296097e073c627dcd0}{int}} $>$}]{new\+Top\+Left\+Position }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

\index{Component@{Component}!setTopRightPosition@{setTopRightPosition}}
\index{setTopRightPosition@{setTopRightPosition}!Component@{Component}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{setTopRightPosition()}{setTopRightPosition()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{png_8h_aa8c59027f9ab2769342f248709d68d17}{void}} Component\+::set\+Top\+Right\+Position (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group__juce__audio__plugin__client-_unity_ga966b05a42d98c7296097e073c627dcd0}{int}}}]{x,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group__juce__audio__plugin__client-_unity_ga966b05a42d98c7296097e073c627dcd0}{int}}}]{y }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Moves the component to a new position.

Changes the position of the component\textquotesingle{}s top-\/right corner (keeping it the same size). The position is relative to the top-\/left of the component\textquotesingle{}s parent.

If the component actually moves, this method will make a synchronous call to \mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_a1b94f2816dc8bc20473620e0db0e8246}{moved()}}.

Note that if you\textquotesingle{}ve used \mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_a42d13229962acb1cdf4328c4a490ffef}{set\+Transform()}} to apply a transform, then the component\textquotesingle{}s bounds will no longer be a direct reflection of the position at which it appears within its parent, as the transform will be applied to whatever bounds you set for it. \mbox{\Hypertarget{class_component_a42d13229962acb1cdf4328c4a490ffef}\label{class_component_a42d13229962acb1cdf4328c4a490ffef}} 
\index{Component@{Component}!setTransform@{setTransform}}
\index{setTransform@{setTransform}!Component@{Component}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{setTransform()}{setTransform()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{png_8h_aa8c59027f9ab2769342f248709d68d17}{void}} Component\+::set\+Transform (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{zconf_8in_8h_a2c212835823e3c54a8ab6d95c652660e}{const}} \mbox{\hyperlink{class_affine_transform}{Affine\+Transform}} \&}]{transform }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Sets a transform matrix to be applied to this component.

If you set a transform for a component, the component\textquotesingle{}s position will be warped by it, relative to the component\textquotesingle{}s parent\textquotesingle{}s top-\/left origin. This means that the values you pass into \mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_a64cbeee83a441e20ed5e7acb600ae107}{set\+Bounds()}} will no longer reflect the actual area within the parent that the component covers, as the bounds will be transformed and the component will probably end up actually appearing somewhere else within its parent.

When using transforms you need to be extremely careful when converting coordinates between the coordinate spaces of different components or the screen -\/ you should always use \mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_a9101a544e864714e0ae0edd4898186bf}{get\+Local\+Point()}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_aca4c6cfd387cd130308bb953def4b7d0}{get\+Local\+Area()}}, etc to do this, and never just manually add a component\textquotesingle{}s position to a point in order to convert it between different components (but I\textquotesingle{}m sure you would never have done that anyway...).

Currently, transforms are not supported for desktop windows, so the transform will be ignored if you put a component on the desktop.

To remove a component\textquotesingle{}s transform, simply pass \mbox{\hyperlink{class_affine_transform}{Affine\+Transform()}} as the parameter to this method. \mbox{\Hypertarget{class_component_aaab69a75feb776176af1395da5dc1ed2}\label{class_component_aaab69a75feb776176af1395da5dc1ed2}} 
\index{Component@{Component}!setViewportIgnoreDragFlag@{setViewportIgnoreDragFlag}}
\index{setViewportIgnoreDragFlag@{setViewportIgnoreDragFlag}!Component@{Component}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{setViewportIgnoreDragFlag()}{setViewportIgnoreDragFlag()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{png_8h_aa8c59027f9ab2769342f248709d68d17}{void}} Component\+::set\+Viewport\+Ignore\+Drag\+Flag (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{bool}]{ignore\+Drag }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}, {\ttfamily [noexcept]}}

Sets a flag to indicate whether mouse drag events on this \mbox{\hyperlink{class_component}{Component}} should be ignored when it is inside a \mbox{\hyperlink{class_viewport}{Viewport}} with drag-\/to-\/scroll functionality enabled. This is useful for Components such as sliders that should not move when their parent \mbox{\hyperlink{class_viewport}{Viewport}} when dragged. \mbox{\Hypertarget{class_component_ac8483af6fe4dc3254e7176df0d8e9f7a}\label{class_component_ac8483af6fe4dc3254e7176df0d8e9f7a}} 
\index{Component@{Component}!setVisible@{setVisible}}
\index{setVisible@{setVisible}!Component@{Component}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{setVisible()}{setVisible()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily virtual \mbox{\hyperlink{png_8h_aa8c59027f9ab2769342f248709d68d17}{void}} Component\+::set\+Visible (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{bool}]{should\+Be\+Visible }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [virtual]}}

Makes the component visible or invisible.

This method will show or hide the component. Note that components default to being non-\/visible when first created. Also note that visible components won\textquotesingle{}t be seen unless all their parent components are also visible.

This method will call \mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_a3859d7aacb18fd51b2fc3e0c51680d1c}{visibility\+Changed()}} and also component\+Visibility\+Changed() for any component listeners that are interested in this component.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em should\+Be\+Visible} & whether to show or hide the component \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\index{Component@{Component}!setWantsKeyboardFocus@{setWantsKeyboardFocus}}
\index{setWantsKeyboardFocus@{setWantsKeyboardFocus}!Component@{Component}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{setWantsKeyboardFocus()}{setWantsKeyboardFocus()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{png_8h_aa8c59027f9ab2769342f248709d68d17}{void}} Component\+::set\+Wants\+Keyboard\+Focus (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{bool}]{wants\+Focus }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [noexcept]}}

Sets a flag to indicate whether this component wants keyboard focus or not.

By default components aren\textquotesingle{}t actually interested in gaining the keyboard focus, but this method can be used to turn this on.

See the \mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_a91886a0e276d27719fa8866a95306571}{grab\+Keyboard\+Focus()}} method for details about the way a component is chosen to receive the focus.

\end{DoxySeeAlso}

\index{Component@{Component}!toBack@{toBack}}
\index{toBack@{toBack}!Component@{Component}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{toBack()}{toBack()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{png_8h_aa8c59027f9ab2769342f248709d68d17}{void}} Component\+::to\+Back (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Changes this component\textquotesingle{}s z-\/order to be at the back of all its siblings.

If the component is set to be \textquotesingle{}always-\/on-\/top\textquotesingle{}, it will only be moved to the back of the other other \textquotesingle{}always-\/on-\/top\textquotesingle{} components.

\index{Component@{Component}!toFront@{toFront}}
\index{toFront@{toFront}!Component@{Component}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{toFront()}{toFront()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{png_8h_aa8c59027f9ab2769342f248709d68d17}{void}} Component\+::to\+Front (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{bool}]{should\+Also\+Gain\+Keyboard\+Focus }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Brings the component to the front of its siblings.

If some of the component\textquotesingle{}s siblings have had their \textquotesingle{}always-\/on-\/top\textquotesingle{} flag set, then they will still be kept in front of this one (unless of course this one is also \textquotesingle{}always-\/on-\/top\textquotesingle{}).


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em should\+Also\+Gain\+Keyboard\+Focus} & if true, this will also try to assign keyboard focus to the component (see \mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_a91886a0e276d27719fa8866a95306571}{grab\+Keyboard\+Focus()}} for more details) \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily static \mbox{\hyperlink{png_8h_aa8c59027f9ab2769342f248709d68d17}{void}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group__juce__core-system_gaf0b3f78ca801d88a7912f4c6bbf50e58}{JUCE\+\_\+\+CALLTYPE}} Component\+::unfocus\+All\+Components (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [static]}}

If any component has keyboard focus, this will defocus it. \mbox{\Hypertarget{class_component_a2d879d2f1eb69e2e828904efc42f0575}\label{class_component_a2d879d2f1eb69e2e828904efc42f0575}} 
\index{Component@{Component}!updateMouseCursor@{updateMouseCursor}}
\index{updateMouseCursor@{updateMouseCursor}!Component@{Component}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{updateMouseCursor()}{updateMouseCursor()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{png_8h_aa8c59027f9ab2769342f248709d68d17}{void}} Component\+::update\+Mouse\+Cursor (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption}) const}

Forces the current mouse cursor to be updated.

If you\textquotesingle{}re overriding the \mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_a712ed320619d48542de733c086f4fd3e}{get\+Mouse\+Cursor()}} method to control which cursor is displayed, then this will only be checked each time the user moves the mouse. So if you want to force the system to check that the cursor being displayed is up-\/to-\/date (even if the mouse is just sitting there), call this method.

(If you\textquotesingle{}re changing the cursor using \mbox{\hyperlink{class_component_ab8c631fc3fb881ca94a9b7edcf58636f}{set\+Mouse\+Cursor()}}, you don\textquotesingle{}t need to bother calling this). \mbox{\Hypertarget{class_component_a543e70d5a3ff75cc3facb476f4cdb131}\label{class_component_a543e70d5a3ff75cc3facb476f4cdb131}} 
\index{Component@{Component}!userTriedToCloseWindow@{userTriedToCloseWindow}}
\index{userTriedToCloseWindow@{userTriedToCloseWindow}!Component@{Component}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{userTriedToCloseWindow()}{userTriedToCloseWindow()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily virtual \mbox{\hyperlink{png_8h_aa8c59027f9ab2769342f248709d68d17}{void}} Component\+::user\+Tried\+To\+Close\+Window (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [virtual]}}

For components on the desktop, this is called if the system wants to close the window.

This is a signal that either the user or the system wants the window to close. The default implementation of this method will trigger an assertion to warn you that your component should do something about it, but you can override this to ignore the event if you want. 

Reimplemented in \mbox{\hyperlink{class_alert_window_ac8263176929ac925f0e4aee768094c55}{Alert\+Window}}, and \mbox{\hyperlink{class_document_window_a056defe79da104beb80243a1416c1f8b}{Document\+Window}}.
